	if now - state.lastSampleTime >= STUCK_CHECK_TIME then
		local moved = (root.Position - state.lastSamplePos).Magnitude
		if moved < STUCK_DISTANCE_THRESHOLD then
			-- flagged as stuck
			if not state.stuckSince then
				state.stuckSince = now
			end
		else
			state.stuckSince = nil
		end
		state.lastSamplePos = root.Position
		state.lastSampleTime = now
	end

	-- If stuck for long enough, try to recover
	if state.stuckSince and (os.clock() - state.stuckSince) > (STUCK_CHECK_TIME * 1.5) then
		state.moveAttempts = (state.moveAttempts or 0) + 1
		if state.moveAttempts <= MAX_MOVE_RETRIES then
			-- retry MoveTo with backoff
			if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] Stuck detected for", npcModel.Name, "retrying MoveTo (attempt)", state.moveAttempts) end

			-- NEW: Fallback PathfindingService Route for Non-Gap Crossings
			-- If we are consistently getting stuck, try to calculate a path around the obstacle
			if state.moveAttempts == 2 and currentWP.type ~= "edge" then
				if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] Attempt 2: Injecting emergency pathfinding to waypoint for " .. npcModel.Name) end
				local emergencyPath = computeWalkablePath(root.Position, waypointPos)
				if #emergencyPath > 0 then
					-- We found a path! Insert these waypoints right before the current one
					for i = #emergencyPath, 1, -1 do
						table.insert(enrichedWaypoints, currentWaypoint, {
							type = "pathfind",
							position = emergencyPath[i],
							tile = currentWP.tile
						})
					end
					-- Reset stuck state to let it follow the new path
					state.stuckSince = nil
					state.moveAttempts = 0
					return
				end
			end

			task.delay(MOVE_RETRY_BACKOFF * state.moveAttempts, function()
				local h = getHumanoid(npcModel)
				if h and npcModel and npcModel.Parent then
					h:MoveTo(waypointPos)
				end
			end)
			-- reset stuck timer to allow the retry to take effect
			state.stuckSince = nil
		else
			-- attempts exhausted -> fallback: either retreat or teleport
			if isRetreat then
				-- if already retreating, teleport directly to origin
				if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] Retreat stuck; teleporting", npcModel.Name) end
				teleportToSafeTile(npcModel)
				stopMovement(npcModel, "Idle")
			else
				if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] Move attempts exhausted; teleporting back to origin for", npcModel.Name) end
				-- teleport to originPosition (safe fallback)
				if movement.originPosition then
					-- try to pivot to origin position (center of origin tile)
					local ok = pcall(function() npcModel:PivotTo(CFrame.new(movement.originPosition)) end)
					if not ok then teleportToSafeTile(npcModel) end
				else
					teleportToSafeTile(npcModel)
				end
				stopMovement(npcModel, "Idle")
			end
		end
	end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- canMoveToTile (unchanged semantics)
---------------------------------------------------

local function canMoveToTile(owner, role, targetTilePart, playerCountry)
	getDependencies()

	local tileCountry = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileCountry(targetTilePart)

	-- Own territory - always allowed
	if tileCountry == playerCountry then
		return true, nil
	end

	-- Already occupied by us - always allowed
	if TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedBy(targetTilePart, owner) then
		return true, nil
	end

	-- Different country
	if tileCountry and tileCountry ~= playerCountry then
		local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
		local tileOwner = CountryOwners[tileCountry]

		-- Conquered territory check
		if type(tileOwner) == "string" and tileOwner:find("Conquered_") then
			local conquerorCountry = tileOwner:gsub("Conquered_", "")
			if conquerorCountry == playerCountry then
				return true, nil
			end
			-- Handle conquered territory owned by someone else
			-- Check if allied with the conqueror
			if DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(playerCountry, conquerorCountry) then
				return true, nil
			end
			-- Defenders cannot move to enemy-conquered territory
			if role == "Defender" then
				return false, "Defenders cannot move to enemy-conquered territory"
			end
			-- Attackers need war with the conqueror to pass
			if not DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(playerCountry, conquerorCountry) then
				return false, "Not at war with " .. conquerorCountry .. " (conqueror of " .. tileCountry .. ")"
			end
			return true, nil
		end

		-- Defenders cannot move to enemy territory
		if role == "Defender" then
			return false, "Defenders cannot move to enemy territory"
		end

		-- For attackers: check war status
		if typeof(tileOwner) == "Instance" and tileOwner:IsA("Player") then
			if not DiplomacyManager.areAtWar(owner, tileOwner) then
				return false, "Not at war with " .. tileCountry
			end
			return true, nil
		elseif tileOwner == "Unowned" then
			-- Allow movement into unowned country territory if at war with it
			if DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(playerCountry, tileCountry) then
				return true, nil
			end
			return false, "Cannot invade neutral territory (" .. tileCountry .. " is unowned)"
		end
	end

	return true, nil
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- startMovement (patched: set up movementState fields + startGroundCheck)
---------------------------------------------------

function NPCMovementSystem.startMovement(npcModel, targetTileKey, targetTilePart)
	getDependencies()

	if not npcModel or not targetTileKey then return false, "Invalid parameters" end

	local owner = Combat.getOwner(npcModel)
	local role = Combat.getRole(npcModel)

	if not owner then return false, "NPC has no owner" end

	if NPCMovementSystem.isRetreating(npcModel) then
		return false, "NPC is retreating"
	end

	if NPCMovementSystem.isMoving(npcModel) then
		stopMovement(npcModel, "Idle")
	end

	local currentTileKey = npcModel:GetAttribute("TileKey")
	if not currentTileKey then
		return false, "NPC has no current tile"
	end

	local resolvedTargetTilePart = targetTilePart
	if not resolvedTargetTilePart then
		resolvedTargetTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(targetTileKey)
		if DEBUG and resolvedTargetTilePart then
			print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] Target tile resolved via getTileFromKey: " .. tostring(targetTileKey) .. " -> " .. resolvedTargetTilePart.Name)
		end
	end
	if not resolvedTargetTilePart then
		resolvedTargetTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKeyWithFallback(targetTileKey)
		if DEBUG then
			if resolvedTargetTilePart then
				print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] WARNING: Target tile resolved via fallback method: " .. tostring(targetTileKey) .. " -> " .. resolvedTargetTilePart.Name)
			else
				print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] ERROR: Target tile FAILED to resolve even with fallback: " .. tostring(targetTileKey))
			end
		end
	end
	if not resolvedTargetTilePart then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] BLOCKED: Cannot resolve target tile " .. tostring(targetTileKey))
		end
		return false, "Invalid target tile"
	end

	local currentTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(currentTileKey)
	-- local currentTileResolutionMethod = "getTileFromKey"
	if currentTilePart and DEBUG then
		print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] Current tile resolved via getTileFromKey: " .. tostring(currentTileKey) .. " -> " .. currentTilePart.Name)
	end
	if not currentTilePart then
		currentTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKeyWithFallback(currentTileKey)
		-- currentTileResolutionMethod = "getTileFromKeyWithFallback"
		if DEBUG then
			if currentTilePart then
				print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] WARNING: Current tile resolved via fallback: " .. tostring(currentTileKey) .. " -> " .. currentTilePart.Name)
			else
				print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] ERROR: Current tile FAILED to resolve even with fallback: " .. tostring(currentTileKey))
			end
		end
	end

	-- local targetTileResolutionMethod = "getTileFromKey"
	if targetTilePart and targetTilePart == resolvedTargetTilePart then
		-- targetTileResolutionMethod = "provided as parameter"
	elseif string.find(tostring(resolvedTargetTilePart), "getTileFromKeyWithFallback") then
		-- targetTileResolutionMethod = "getTileFromKeyWithFallback"
	end

	-- Validate NPC is actually near its resolved tile (defense-in-depth for TileKey mismatch)
	if currentTilePart then
		local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
		if root then
			local npcPosXZ = root.Position * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)
			local tilePosXZ = currentTilePart.Position * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)
			local tileDistance = (npcPosXZ - tilePosXZ).Magnitude

			if tileDistance > currentTilePart.Size.Magnitude / 2 + 5 then
				local correctedTile = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileUnderPosition(root.Position)
				if correctedTile then
					if DEBUG then
						print("[NPCMovement:Resolution] TileKey mismatch corrected: " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " -> " .. correctedTile.Name .. " (NPC was " .. math.floor(tileDistance) .. " studs away)")
					end
					currentTilePart = correctedTile
					local correctedKey = TileManager.getTileKeyFromPart(correctedTile)
					if correctedKey then
						currentTileKey = correctedKey
						npcModel:SetAttribute("TileKey", correctedKey)
					end
					-- Fix C: Update CurrentTileId to match the corrected tile
					local correctedTileId = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileId(correctedTile)
					if correctedTileId then
						npcModel:SetAttribute("CurrentTileId", correctedTileId)
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end

	-- STRICT VALIDATION: Reject movement if current tile fails to resolve properly
	-- This prevents using the weaker key-based fallback adjacency check
	if not currentTilePart then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] BLOCKED: Current tile failed to resolve: " .. tostring(currentTileKey))
		end
		return false, "Cannot determine current tile position"
	end

	-- FIX: Use ONLY the reliable rasterization-based method, never fallback to weaker key-based method
	-- The key-based method uses raycast fallback which can return incorrect tiles on irregular terrain
	if not currentTilePart or not resolvedTargetTilePart then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] BLOCKED: Cannot use reliable adjacency check - tile parts not properly resolved")
			if not currentTilePart then
				print("  - Current tile failed to resolve: " .. tostring(currentTileKey))
			end
			if not resolvedTargetTilePart then
				print("  - Target tile failed to resolve: " .. tostring(targetTileKey))
			end
		end
		return false, "Cannot determine if tiles are adjacent - resolution failed"
	end

	-- If tiles are directly adjacent, use direct 2-tile path (skip BFS)
	-- This prevents routing through intermediate tiles when the destination is right next door.
	-- Diplomacy/occupancy for the destination is checked separately by canMoveToTile below.
	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(owner)
	local areTilesDirectlyAdjacent = TileAdjacencyManager.areTilesAdjacent(currentTilePart, resolvedTargetTilePart)
	local tilePath
	local excludedEdges = {}  -- Per-move exclusion set

	if areTilesDirectlyAdjacent then
		tilePath = {currentTilePart, resolvedTargetTilePart}
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement:Pathfinding] Direct adjacent move: " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " -> " .. resolvedTargetTilePart.Name)
		end
	else
		-- Multi-tile pathfinding with diplomacy validation (for non-adjacent destinations)
		tilePath = findTilePath(currentTilePart, resolvedTargetTilePart, nil, owner, role, playerCountry, excludedEdges)
	end

	if not tilePath then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] No path found from " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " to " .. resolvedTargetTilePart.Name)
		end
		return false, "Cannot reach target tile"
	end

	if DEBUG and not areTilesDirectlyAdjacent then
		local pathStr = currentTilePart.Name
		for i = 2, #tilePath do
			pathStr = pathStr .. " -> " .. tilePath[i].Name
		end
		print("[NPCMovement:Pathfinding] Found path: " .. pathStr)
	end

	-- For direct-adjacent moves, verify a walkable crossing proof exists before committing.
	-- This catches adjacency-table false positives that would otherwise send NPCs into walls.
	if areTilesDirectlyAdjacent then
		local proof = TileAdjacencyManager.getAdjacencyProof(currentTilePart, resolvedTargetTilePart)
		if not proof then
			if DEBUG then
				warn("[NPCMovement] No adjacency proof for direct move: " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " -> " .. resolvedTargetTilePart.Name .. " — blocking movement")
			end
			return false, "No walkable crossing between tiles"
		end
	end

	-- playerCountry already defined above for pathfinding
	local canMove, moveError = canMoveToTile(owner, role, resolvedTargetTilePart, playerCountry)
	if not canMove then
		return false, moveError
	end

	-- Occupancy check.
	-- resolvedTargetTilePart is already available; resolve TileId directly (no key roundtrip).
	local startMoveTileId = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileId(resolvedTargetTilePart)
	local currentOccupant = TileManager.getTileOccupantById(startMoveTileId)
	if currentOccupant and currentOccupant ~= npcModel then
		return false, "Tile is occupied by another NPC"
	end

	-- Reservation check - ALLOW competitive movement
	-- We check if reserved, but we DO NOT stop movement. 
	-- Multiple NPCs can now race to the same tile.
	if isTileReservedByOther(targetTileKey, npcModel) then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] " .. npcModel.Name .. " represents a race condition: moving to reserved tile " .. targetTileKey)
		end
		-- PROCEED anyway, do not return false
	end

	-- Try to reserve, but process even if failed (competitive)
	if not reserveTile(targetTileKey, npcModel) then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[NPCMovement] Could not reserve " .. targetTileKey .. " (likely taken), but moving anyway")
		end
		-- Continue to move even if reservation failed
	end

	-- Positions
	local targetPosition = getTileSpawnPosition(resolvedTargetTilePart)
	local originTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(currentTileKey)
	if not originTilePart then
		local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
		if root then
			originTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileUnderPosition(root.Position)
		end
	end
	local originPosition = originTilePart and getTileSpawnPosition(originTilePart) or getRootPart(npcModel).Position
	if not targetPosition then
		releaseTileReservation(targetTileKey, npcModel)
		return false, "Could not calculate target position"
	end

	-- Set up movement state
	movementStates[npcModel] = movementStates[npcModel] or {}
	movementStates[npcModel].state = "Moving"
	movementStates[npcModel].lastTeleport = movementStates[npcModel].lastTeleport or 0
	movementStates[npcModel].lastSamplePos = getRootPart(npcModel) and getRootPart(npcModel).Position or Vector3.new(0,0,0)
	movementStates[npcModel].lastSampleTime = os.clock()
	movementStates[npcModel].stuckSince = nil
	movementStates[npcModel].moveAttempts = 0
	movementStates[npcModel].fallRecoveries = 0  -- Reset fall recovery counter on new movement

	-- Mark as moving and disable the Health regeneration script for the duration
	npcModel:SetAttribute("IsMoving", true)
	setNPCHealthScriptEnabled(npcModel, false)

	-- Build enriched waypoints with edge-crossing points for gap tiles
	local enrichedWaypoints, directEdgeFailed = buildEnrichedWaypoints(tilePath, excludedEdges)

	-- Adjacent tiles must cross their shared border directly (no intermediate routing).
	-- The adjacency invariant guarantees a walkable crossing existed at init time.
	-- getBestWalkableBorderCrossing retries with k=5 candidates at runtime.

	if not enrichedWaypoints or #enrichedWaypoints < 2 then
		releaseTileReservation(targetTileKey, npcModel)
		return false, "Failed to build waypoints"
	end

	activeMovements[npcModel] = {
		targetTileKey = targetTileKey,
		originTileKey = currentTileKey,
		targetPosition = targetPosition,
		originPosition = originPosition,
		tilePath = tilePath,                    -- keep original for reference
		enrichedWaypoints = enrichedWaypoints,  -- enriched path with edge-crossing points
		currentWaypoint = 2,                    -- index into enrichedWaypoints (skip first)
		connection = nil
	}

	-- Move to the first enriched waypoint position
	local firstWaypointPos = enrichedWaypoints[2].position

	local humanoid = getHumanoid(npcModel)
	if humanoid and firstWaypointPos then
		humanoid:MoveTo(firstWaypointPos)
	end

	-- monitor loop
	local connection
	connection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not npcModel or not npcModel.Parent then
			pcall(function() connection:Disconnect() end)
			return
		end
		monitorMovement(npcModel, false)
	end)
	activeMovements[npcModel].connection = connection

	-- start ground check
	startGroundCheck(npcModel)

	if DEBUG then
		print("[NPCMovement] " .. npcModel.Name .. " moving from " .. currentTileKey .. " to " .. targetTileKey)
		makeDebugPart("MoveTarget_"..npcModel.Name, targetPosition + Vector3.new(0,1,0), Vector3.new(0.8,0.8,0.8), Color3.fromRGB(0,150,255), 2)
	end

	return true
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- startRetreat (patched: release & reset state)
---------------------------------------------------

function NPCMovementSystem.startRetreat(npcModel, originTileKey, originPosition)
	getDependencies()

	if not npcModel then return end

	local movement = activeMovements[npcModel]
	if movement then
		if movement.targetTileKey then releaseTileReservation(movement.targetTileKey, npcModel) end
		if movement.connection then pcall(function() movement.connection:Disconnect() end) end
	end

	movementStates[npcModel] = movementStates[npcModel] or {}
	movementStates[npcModel].state = "Retreating"
	movementStates[npcModel].moveAttempts = 0
	movementStates[npcModel].stuckSince = nil

	local tileKey = originTileKey or npcModel:GetAttribute("TileKey")
	local tilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(tileKey)
	local targetPos = originPosition or (tilePart and getTileSpawnPosition(tilePart))

	if not targetPos then
		local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
		if root then targetPos = root.Position else stopMovement(npcModel, "Idle"); return end
	end

	activeMovements[npcModel] = {
		targetTileKey = tileKey,
		originTileKey = tileKey,
		targetPosition = targetPos,
		originPosition = targetPos,
		enrichedWaypoints = {
			{ type = "tile", position = targetPos, tile = tilePart },
			{ type = "tile", position = targetPos, tile = tilePart }
		},
		currentWaypoint = 2,
		connection = nil
	}

	local humanoid = getHumanoid(npcModel)
	if humanoid then humanoid:MoveTo(targetPos) end

	local connection
	connection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not npcModel or not npcModel.Parent then pcall(function() connection:Disconnect() end); return end
		monitorMovement(npcModel, true)
	end)
	activeMovements[npcModel].connection = connection

	if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] " .. npcModel.Name .. " retreating (invulnerable)") end
end

function NPCMovementSystem.cancelMovement(npcModel)
	if NPCMovementSystem.isRetreating(npcModel) then
		return false
	end
	stopMovement(npcModel, "Idle")
	return true
end

function NPCMovementSystem.restoreToMovementOrigin(npcModel)
	getDependencies()

	if not npcModel then
		return false, "Invalid NPC"
	end

	if NPCMovementSystem.isRetreating(npcModel) then
		return false, "NPC is retreating"
	end

	local movement = activeMovements[npcModel]
	if not movement then
		return false, "NPC has no active movement"
	end

	local originTileKey = movement.originTileKey or npcModel:GetAttribute("TileKey")
	local originTilePart = originTileKey and TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(originTileKey) or nil
	local originPosition = movement.originPosition or (originTilePart and getTileSpawnPosition(originTilePart))

	if movement.targetTileKey then
		releaseTileReservation(movement.targetTileKey, npcModel)
	end

	if movement.connection then
		pcall(function() movement.connection:Disconnect() end)
	end

	activeMovements[npcModel] = nil

	movementStates[npcModel] = movementStates[npcModel] or {}
	movementStates[npcModel].state = "Idle"
	movementStates[npcModel].moveAttempts = 0
	movementStates[npcModel].stuckSince = nil
	movementStates[npcModel].lastStopTime = os.clock()
	movementStates[npcModel].lastSamplePos = originPosition or (getRootPart(npcModel) and getRootPart(npcModel).Position) or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	movementStates[npcModel].lastSampleTime = os.clock()

	if originTileKey then
		npcModel:SetAttribute("TileKey", originTileKey)
	end

	if originTilePart then
		local originTileId = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileId(originTilePart)
		if originTileId then
			npcModel:SetAttribute("CurrentTileId", originTileId)
		end
	end

	if originPosition then
		pcall(function() npcModel:PivotTo(CFrame.new(originPosition)) end)
	end

	local restoreHumanoid = getHumanoid(npcModel)
	local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
	if restoreHumanoid then
		if originPosition then
			restoreHumanoid:MoveTo(originPosition)
		elseif root then
			restoreHumanoid:MoveTo(root.Position)
		end
	end

	npcModel:SetAttribute("IsMoving", nil)
	if Combat and not Combat.isInCombat(npcModel) then
		setNPCHealthScriptEnabled(npcModel, true)
	end

	return true, originTileKey
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- OnOwnerChanged: reset movement state when ownership transfers
---------------------------------------------------

function NPCMovementSystem.OnOwnerChanged(npcModel)
	if not npcModel then return end
	movementStates[npcModel] = movementStates[npcModel] or {}
	movementStates[npcModel].state = "Idle"
	movementStates[npcModel].stuckSince = nil
	movementStates[npcModel].moveAttempts = 0

	for k, v in pairs(reservedTiles) do
		if v == npcModel then reservedTiles[k] = nil end
	end

	local ownerChangeMovement = activeMovements[npcModel]
	if ownerChangeMovement and ownerChangeMovement.connection then
		pcall(function() ownerChangeMovement.connection:Disconnect() end)
	end
	activeMovements[npcModel] = nil

	if DEBUG then print("[NPCMovement] OnOwnerChanged: reset movement state for", npcModel.Name) end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Cleanup
---------------------------------------------------

function NPCMovementSystem.unregisterNPC(npcModel)
	-- Clean up ground check
	if groundCheckConnections[npcModel] then
		groundCheckConnections[npcModel]:Disconnect()
		groundCheckConnections[npcModel] = nil
	end

	-- Clean up movement & reservations
	local movement = activeMovements[npcModel]
	if movement and movement.targetTileKey then
		releaseTileReservation(movement.targetTileKey, npcModel)
	end

	stopMovement(npcModel, nil)
	movementStates[npcModel] = nil
	activeMovements[npcModel] = nil
end

-- Watch for NPC removals via Tag
-- Initialize logic
local function init()
	local NPC_TAG = "RegisteredNPC"

	-- Handle removals
	CollectionService:GetInstanceRemovedSignal(NPC_TAG):Connect(function(child)
		if movementStates[child] or groundCheckConnections[child] then
			NPCMovementSystem.unregisterNPC(child)
		end
	end)

	-- Handle existing
	for _, child in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged(NPC_TAG)) do
		startGroundCheck(child)
	end

	-- Handle additions
	CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal(NPC_TAG):Connect(function(child)
		-- Wait for components to replicate/initialize
		task.defer(function()
			local humanoid = child:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 1)
			local ownerVal  = child:WaitForChild("NPCOwner",  1)
			if not child.Parent then return end  -- destroyed during the wait
			if not humanoid or not ownerVal then
				warn("[NPCMovement] NPC missing Humanoid/NPCOwner after 1s:", child.Name)
				return
			end
			startGroundCheck(child)
		end)
	end)
end

-- Run init
task.spawn(init)

return NPCMovementSystem

--- src/shared/NPCCombatSystem.luau ---
-- Module: NPCCombatSystem (COUNTRY PERSISTENCE VERSION)
-- NPCs can now be transferred between players when countries change hands
-- Country-owned NPCs (no active player) remain idle until claimed
-- Combat requires tile adjacency - NPCs can only attack enemies on adjacent tiles
-- Uses DiplomacyManager.canAttack() which checks both war AND alliance status
-- Maid-owned lifecycle signals, idempotent registerNPC, ordered unregisterNPC,
-- NPCMovementSystem.OnOwnerChanged wired into transferOwnership

local PathfindingService = game:GetService("PathfindingService")
local Debris = game:GetService("Debris")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local DiplomacyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("DiplomacyManager", 10))

local Combat = {}

-- Lazy-load TileAdjacencyManager to avoid circular dependency
local TileAdjacencyManager = nil
local function getTileAdjacencyManager()
	if not TileAdjacencyManager then
		TileAdjacencyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileAdjacencyManager", 10))
	end
	return TileAdjacencyManager
end

-- Lazy-load TileOwnershipManager to avoid circular dependency
local TileOwnershipManager = nil
local function getTileOwnershipManager()
	if not TileOwnershipManager then
		TileOwnershipManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileOwnershipManager", 10))
	end
	return TileOwnershipManager
end

-- Lazy-load NPCMovementSystem to avoid circular dependency
local NPCMovementSystem = nil
local function getNPCMovementSystem()
	if not NPCMovementSystem then
		NPCMovementSystem = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("NPCMovementSystem", 10))
	end
	return NPCMovementSystem
end

-- Config
local SHOOT_INTERVAL = 1
local DAMAGE = 10
local BEAM_LIFETIME = 0.1
local LOOP_WAIT = 0.1
local PATH_RECALC_COOLDOWN = 1.0
local DEBUG = true

-- Server Owner folder for server-owned NPCs
local SERVER_OWNER = Instance.new("Folder")
SERVER_OWNER.Name = "ServerOwner"
SERVER_OWNER.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Internal tables
local npcOwners = {}
local npcRoles = {}
local combatLoops = {}   -- [npcModel] = token (unique table reference per loop instance)
local npcCooldown = {}
local defenderAttackers = {}  -- Tracks who is attacking each Defender
local attackerThreats = {}    -- Tracks who is attacking each Attacker (for auto-retaliation)
local pathTimestamps = {}
local debugParts = {}
local npcInCombat = {}  -- npcModel -> bool: tracks active combat state for Health script management

-- Manual targets: stores a LIST of targets for each attacker
-- manualTargets[npcModel] = { targetModel1, targetModel2, ... }
local manualTargets = {}

-- Per-NPC runtime state bag, owns all lifecycle signals via the Maid.
-- npcRuntime[npcModel] = { maid = Maid }
local npcRuntime = {}

---------------------------------------------------
-- Private: Lightweight Maid / Janitor
-- Owns per-NPC signals and cleanup callbacks.
-- DoCleaning() disconnects all connections, calls all callbacks, then clears the task list.
---------------------------------------------------

local function newMaid()
	local maid = { _tasks = {} }

	function maid:Give(task)
		table.insert(self._tasks, task)
		return task
	end

	function maid:DoCleaning()
		for _, task in ipairs(self._tasks) do
			if typeof(task) == "RBXScriptConnection" then
				task:Disconnect()
			elseif typeof(task) == "function" then
				task()
			elseif typeof(task) == "Instance" then
				task:Destroy()
			end
		end
		table.clear(self._tasks)
	end

	return maid
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Utilities
---------------------------------------------------

local function getRootPart(model)
	if not model then return nil end
	return model:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or model:FindFirstChild("Torso") or model.PrimaryPart
end

local function cleanupDebugParts(modelName)
	if not DEBUG then return end

	local targetKey = modelName .. "_Target"
	if debugParts[targetKey] then
		debugParts[targetKey]:Destroy()
		debugParts[targetKey] = nil
	end

	for key, part in pairs(debugParts) do
		if string.find(key, modelName .. "_Path_") then
			if part and part.Parent then
				part:Destroy()
			end
			debugParts[key] = nil
		end
	end
end

-- Register Humanoid.Died cleanup through the NPC's maid so there is no hidden ownership.
local function setupDeathCleanup(npcModel, maid)
	local humanoid = npcModel:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	if not humanoid then return end

	maid:Give(humanoid.Died:Once(function()
		Combat.clearAllManualTargets(npcModel)
		Combat.unregisterNPC(npcModel)
		Debris:AddItem(npcModel, 0.5)
	end))
end

-- Enable or disable the Health regeneration script inside an NPC model
local function setHealthScriptEnabled(npcModel, enabled)
	if not npcModel then return end
	local healthScript = npcModel:FindFirstChild("Health", true)
	if healthScript and (healthScript:IsA("Script") or healthScript:IsA("LocalScript")) then
		healthScript.Enabled = enabled
		if DEBUG then
			print("[Combat] Health script " .. (enabled and "enabled" or "disabled") .. " for " .. npcModel.Name)
		end
	end
end

-- Update the NPC's combat state and manage its Health script accordingly.
-- Called each combat-loop iteration with the current count of valid targets.
local function updateCombatHealthState(npcModel, inCombat)
	if npcInCombat[npcModel] == inCombat then return end  -- State unchanged; skip
	npcInCombat[npcModel] = inCombat
	if inCombat then
		-- Entering combat: always disable the Health script
		setHealthScriptEnabled(npcModel, false)
	else
		-- Leaving combat: re-enable Health only when the NPC is also not moving
		local isMoving = npcModel:GetAttribute("IsMoving") == true
		if not isMoving then
			setHealthScriptEnabled(npcModel, true)
		end
	end
end

local function drawDebugLine(name, startPos, endPos, color, lifetime)
	if not DEBUG then return end

	local distance = (endPos - startPos).Magnitude
	local beam = debugParts[name]
	if not beam or not beam.Parent then
		beam = Instance.new("Part")
		debugParts[name] = beam
	end

	beam.Name = name
	beam.Anchored = true
	beam.CanCollide = false
	beam.CastShadow = false
	beam.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
	beam.Color = color
	beam.Size = Vector3.new(0.2, 0.2, distance)
	beam.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(startPos, endPos) * CFrame.new(0, 0, -distance / 2)

	if not beam.Parent then
		beam.Parent = workspace
	end

	if lifetime then
		task.delay(lifetime, function()
			if debugParts[name] == beam then
				debugParts[name] = nil
			end
		end)
		Debris:AddItem(beam, lifetime)
	end

	return beam
end

local function createLaserBeam(originPos, targetPos, color)
	local distance = (targetPos - originPos).Magnitude
	local beam = Instance.new("Part")
	beam.Anchored = true
	beam.CanCollide = false
	beam.CastShadow = false
	beam.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
	beam.Color = color or Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
	beam.Size = Vector3.new(0.2, 0.2, distance)
	beam.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(originPos, targetPos) * CFrame.new(0, 0, -distance / 2)
	beam.Parent = workspace
	Debris:AddItem(beam, BEAM_LIFETIME)
end

-- Multi-target fire with split damage
local function fireMultiLaser(npcModel, targetHumanoids, beamColor)
	if not npcModel or #targetHumanoids == 0 then return end

	local npcRoot = getRootPart(npcModel)
	if not npcRoot then return end

	-- Split damage evenly among all targets
	local damagePerTarget = DAMAGE / #targetHumanoids

	for _, targetHumanoid in ipairs(targetHumanoids) do
		if targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 then
			local targetRoot = getRootPart(targetHumanoid.Parent)
			if targetRoot then
				createLaserBeam(npcRoot.Position, targetRoot.Position, beamColor)
				targetHumanoid:TakeDamage(damagePerTarget)
				-- Auto-retaliation: notify target it was hit (only triggers for AutoRetaliate NPCs)
				local targetNpcModel = targetHumanoid.Parent
				if targetNpcModel then
					Combat.noteHit(npcModel, targetNpcModel)
				end
				if DEBUG then
					print(npcModel.Name, "SPLIT FIRE at", targetHumanoid.Parent.Name, "for", string.format("%.2f", damagePerTarget), "damage")
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

local function visualizePath(path, modelName)
	if not DEBUG then return end

	for key, part in pairs(debugParts) do
		if string.find(key, modelName .. "_Path_") then
			if part and part.Parent then
				part:Destroy()
			end
			debugParts[key] = nil
		end
	end

	local waypoints = path:GetWaypoints()
	for i = 1, #waypoints - 1 do
		local startPos = waypoints[i].Position
		local endPos = waypoints[i+1].Position
		drawDebugLine(modelName .. "_Path_" .. i, startPos, endPos, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0), PATH_RECALC_COOLDOWN + 0.1)
	end
end

-- Helper to check if NPC has an active player owner
local function hasActivePlayerOwner(npcModel)
	local currentOwner = Combat.getOwner(npcModel)
	return currentOwner and typeof(currentOwner) == "Instance" and currentOwner:IsA("Player") and currentOwner.Parent
end

-- Check if two NPCs are on adjacent tiles
local function areNPCsOnAdjacentTiles(npcA, npcB)
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	return TAM.canNPCsInteract(npcA, npcB)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Combat Loops
-- Each loop instance is identified by a unique token stored in combatLoops[npcModel].
-- The loop exits when the token changes (re-registration) or when the NPC dies/is removed.
---------------------------------------------------

-- Shared combat loop for both Attackers and Defenders (multi-target with split damage + adjacency check).
-- beamColor distinguishes the role visually (red for Attackers, blue for Defenders).
local function startCombatLoop(npcModel, getAllTargets, beamColor)
	if not npcModel then return end
	if combatLoops[npcModel] then return end

	-- Use a unique table reference as a generation token.
	-- When re-registration nils combatLoops[npcModel], this loop detects the token mismatch and exits.
	local token = {}
	combatLoops[npcModel] = token

	task.spawn(function()
		local humanoid = npcModel:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

		while combatLoops[npcModel] == token and npcModel.Parent and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 do
			local now = os.clock()

			local allTargets = getAllTargets()

			-- Sync Health script with current combat state
			updateCombatHealthState(npcModel, #allTargets > 0)

			-- Only go idle if country-owned AND no targets/threats
			if not hasActivePlayerOwner(npcModel) and #allTargets == 0 then
				local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
				if root then
					humanoid:MoveTo(root.Position)
				end
				task.wait(LOOP_WAIT)
				continue
			end

			if #allTargets > 0 then
				local npcRoot = getRootPart(npcModel)

				if npcRoot then
					-- Stop movement
					humanoid:MoveTo(npcRoot.Position)

					-- Face the first target
					local firstTarget = allTargets[1]
					if firstTarget and firstTarget.Parent then
						local targetRoot = getRootPart(firstTarget.Parent)
						if targetRoot then
							local targetPos = targetRoot.Position
							local selfPos = npcRoot.Position
							local lookAtCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(
								selfPos,
								Vector3.new(targetPos.X, selfPos.Y, targetPos.Z)
							)
							npcRoot.CFrame = CFrame.new(npcRoot.CFrame.Position) * (lookAtCFrame - lookAtCFrame.Position)
						end
					end

					-- Fire at all targets with split damage
					if #allTargets > 0 then
						local lastShot = npcCooldown[npcModel] or 0
						if now - lastShot >= SHOOT_INTERVAL then
							fireMultiLaser(npcModel, allTargets, beamColor)
							npcCooldown[npcModel] = now
						end
					end
				end
			else
				-- No targets - idle
				if DEBUG then
					local targetKey = npcModel.Name .. "_Target"
					if debugParts[targetKey] then
						debugParts[targetKey]:Destroy()
						debugParts[targetKey] = nil
					end
				end
				local root = getRootPart(npcModel)
				if root then
					humanoid:MoveTo(root.Position)
				end
			end

			task.wait(LOOP_WAIT)
		end

		-- Only unregister if we are still the active loop instance and the NPC is gone.
		-- Token mismatch means we were superseded by a re-registration — exit silently.
		if combatLoops[npcModel] == token and not npcModel.Parent then
			Combat.unregisterNPC(npcModel)
		end
	end)
end

-- Thin wrapper: starts the combat loop with red beams for Attackers.
local function startAttackerCombatLoop(npcModel, getAllTargets)
	startCombatLoop(npcModel, getAllTargets, Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0))
end

-- Thin wrapper: starts the combat loop with blue beams for Defenders.
local function startDefenderCombatLoop(npcModel, getAllTargets)
	startCombatLoop(npcModel, getAllTargets, Color3.fromRGB(0, 150, 255))
end

-- Public API

function Combat.getServerOwner()
	return SERVER_OWNER
end

-- Transfer ownership of an NPC to a new player (or nil for country-owned).
-- Resets movement state via NPCMovementSystem.OnOwnerChanged.
function Combat.transferOwnership(npcModel, newOwner)
	if not npcModel then return false end

	local oldOwner = npcOwners[npcModel]
	npcOwners[npcModel] = newOwner

	-- Clear manual targets when ownership changes
	Combat.clearAllManualTargets(npcModel)

	-- Clear from defender/attacker threat lists (this NPC's own lists)
	defenderAttackers[npcModel] = nil
	attackerThreats[npcModel] = nil

	-- FIX: Also remove this NPC from OTHER NPCs' target/threat lists
	-- This prevents combat bugs when ownership changes
	for otherNPC, targets in pairs(manualTargets) do
		for i = #targets, 1, -1 do
			if targets[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(targets, i)
			end
		end
	end

	for defender, attackers in pairs(defenderAttackers) do
		for i = #attackers, 1, -1 do
			if attackers[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(attackers, i)
			end
		end
	end

	for attacker, threats in pairs(attackerThreats) do
		for i = #threats, 1, -1 do
			if threats[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(threats, i)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Reset movement state after ownership change so the NPC cannot retain:
	-- active movement monitor, stale reservation, retreat state, or stale IsMoving.
	local moveSystem = getNPCMovementSystem()
	if moveSystem and moveSystem.OnOwnerChanged then
		moveSystem.OnOwnerChanged(npcModel)
	end

	if DEBUG then
		local oldName = oldOwner and (typeof(oldOwner) == "Instance" and oldOwner.Name or "Unknown") or "None"
		local newName = newOwner and (typeof(newOwner) == "Instance" and newOwner.Name or "Unknown") or "Country-Owned"
		print("[Combat] Transferred " .. npcModel.Name .. " from " .. oldName .. " to " .. newName)
	end

	return true
end

-- Add a target to an attacker's target list
function Combat.addManualTarget(attackerModel, targetModel)
	if not attackerModel or not targetModel then return false end

	if not manualTargets[attackerModel] then
		manualTargets[attackerModel] = {}
	end

	-- Check for duplicates
	for _, existing in ipairs(manualTargets[attackerModel]) do
		if existing == targetModel then
			if DEBUG then
				print("[Combat] " .. targetModel.Name .. " already in " .. attackerModel.Name .. "'s target list")
			end
			return false -- Already targeting
		end
	end

	table.insert(manualTargets[attackerModel], targetModel)

	if DEBUG then
		print("[Combat] " .. attackerModel.Name .. " now targeting " .. #manualTargets[attackerModel] .. " enemy(s)")
	end

	return true -- Successfully added
end

-- Remove a specific target from an attacker's target list
function Combat.removeManualTarget(attackerModel, targetModel)
	if not attackerModel or not targetModel then return false end

	local targets = manualTargets[attackerModel]
	if not targets then return false end

	for i, existing in ipairs(targets) do
		if existing == targetModel then
			table.remove(targets, i)

			-- Reciprocal cleanup: remove attackerModel from the target's tracking list
			local targetRole = npcRoles[targetModel]
			if targetRole == "Defender" then
				Combat.removeAttackerFromDefender(attackerModel, targetModel)
			elseif targetRole == "Attacker" then
				Combat.removeThreatFromAttacker(attackerModel, targetModel)
			end

			if DEBUG then
				print("[Combat] " .. targetModel.Name .. " removed from " .. attackerModel.Name .. "'s targets")
			end
			return true
		end
	end

	return false
end

-- Clear all manual targets and clean up reciprocal tracking lists
function Combat.clearAllManualTargets(attackerModel)
	if not attackerModel then return end

	local targets = manualTargets[attackerModel]
	if targets then
		for _, target in ipairs(targets) do
			if target then
				local targetRole = npcRoles[target]
				if targetRole == "Defender" then
					Combat.removeAttackerFromDefender(attackerModel, target)
				elseif targetRole == "Attacker" then
					Combat.removeThreatFromAttacker(attackerModel, target)
				end
			end
		end
	end

	manualTargets[attackerModel] = nil
end

-- Get all manual targets for an attacker
function Combat.getManualTargets(attackerModel)
	return manualTargets[attackerModel] or {}
end

-- Get count of manual targets
function Combat.getManualTargetCount(attackerModel)
	local targets = manualTargets[attackerModel]
	return targets and #targets or 0
end

-- LEGACY: For backwards compatibility (sets single target, clearing others)
function Combat.setManualTarget(attackerModel, targetModel)
	Combat.clearAllManualTargets(attackerModel)
	if targetModel then
		Combat.addManualTarget(attackerModel, targetModel)
	end
end

-- LEGACY: Get first manual target (for backwards compatibility)
function Combat.getManualTarget(attackerModel)
	local targets = manualTargets[attackerModel]
	return targets and targets[1] or nil
end

-- LEGACY: Clear manual target
function Combat.clearManualTarget(attackerModel)
	Combat.clearAllManualTargets(attackerModel)
end

-- Register an NPC with the combat system.
-- Idempotent: calling this on an already-registered NPC cleans the old maid first,
-- then creates a fresh maid and re-registers all signals. No duplicate callbacks.
function Combat.registerNPC(npcModel, ownerPlayer, role)
	if not npcModel or not role then return end

	-- Idempotency: if already registered, clean the old lifecycle signals.
	-- This clears old Destroying and Died connections but does NOT nil the combat tables —
	-- the NPC is alive and should retain its external targeting state.
	if npcRuntime[npcModel] then
		npcRuntime[npcModel].maid:DoCleaning()
		npcRuntime[npcModel] = nil
		-- Nil the loop token so startAttackerCombatLoop / startDefenderCombatLoop can run fresh.
		-- The old loop will detect the token mismatch on its next iteration and exit cleanly.
		combatLoops[npcModel] = nil
	end

	-- Create fresh maid and runtime bag
	local maid = newMaid()
	npcRuntime[npcModel] = { maid = maid }

	-- Register Destroying through maid (replaces bare .Destroying:Connect)
	maid:Give(npcModel.Destroying:Connect(function()
		Combat.clearAllManualTargets(npcModel)
		Combat.unregisterNPC(npcModel)
	end))

	-- Register Humanoid.Died through maid (replaces setupDeathCleanup's hidden ownership)
	setupDeathCleanup(npcModel, maid)

	-- Update owner/role tables
	npcOwners[npcModel] = ownerPlayer
	npcRoles[npcModel] = role

	if role == "Attacker" then
		-- Attackers use multi-target combat with manually assigned targets + auto-retaliation
		startAttackerCombatLoop(npcModel, function()
			local allValidTargets = {}

			-- Get all manual targets
			local targets = manualTargets[npcModel] or {}

			-- Validate and collect humanoids, remove dead/invalid/non-adjacent targets
			for i = #targets, 1, -1 do
				local target = targets[i]

				if target and target.Parent then
					local targetHumanoid = target:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

					-- Check tile adjacency
					local isAdjacent = areNPCsOnAdjacentTiles(npcModel, target)

					-- Use country-based check so country-owned (nil-owner) NPCs are handled correctly
					local canFight = DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(npcModel, target)

					if targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 and canFight and isAdjacent then
						table.insert(allValidTargets, targetHumanoid)
					else
						-- Invalid target (friendly, allied, not at war, dead, or not adjacent), remove it
						table.remove(targets, i)
						if DEBUG then
							local reason = not isAdjacent and "not adjacent" or (not canFight and "not at war/allied" or "invalid")
							print("[Combat] " .. npcModel.Name .. " removed " .. reason .. " manual target")
						end
					end
				else
					-- Target destroyed, remove it
					table.remove(targets, i)
				end
			end

			-- Only include threats for COUNTRY-OWNED attackers (auto-retaliation)
			-- Player-owned attackers should only attack their manual targets
			if not hasActivePlayerOwner(npcModel) then
				local threats = attackerThreats[npcModel] or {}
				for i = #threats, 1, -1 do
					local threat = threats[i]

					if threat and threat.Parent then
						local threatHumanoid = threat:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

						-- Check tile adjacency for threats
						local isAdjacent = areNPCsOnAdjacentTiles(npcModel, threat)

						-- Use country-based check so country-owned (nil-owner) NPCs are handled correctly
						local canFight = DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(npcModel, threat)

						if threatHumanoid and threatHumanoid.Health > 0 and canFight and isAdjacent then
							-- Check if not already in targets list
							local alreadyTargeted = false
							for _, existing in ipairs(allValidTargets) do
								if existing == threatHumanoid then
									alreadyTargeted = true
									break
								end
							end
							if not alreadyTargeted then
								table.insert(allValidTargets, threatHumanoid)
							end
						else
							-- Invalid threat (not adjacent or other reason), remove it
							table.remove(threats, i)
						end
					else
						-- Threat destroyed, remove it
						table.remove(threats, i)
					end
				end
			end

			return allValidTargets
		end)
	else -- Defender
		-- Defenders use multi-target combat with auto-retaliation
		startDefenderCombatLoop(npcModel, function()
			local allValidTargets = {}

			local attackers = defenderAttackers[npcModel] or {}

			for i = #attackers, 1, -1 do
				local att = attackers[i]

				if att and att.Parent then
					local attHumanoid = att:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
					local isAdjacent = areNPCsOnAdjacentTiles(npcModel, att)
					local canFight = DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(npcModel, att)
					if attHumanoid and attHumanoid.Health > 0 and canFight and isAdjacent then
						table.insert(allValidTargets, attHumanoid)
					else
						table.remove(attackers, i)
					end
				else
					table.remove(attackers, i)
				end
			end

			return allValidTargets
		end)
	end

	if DEBUG then
		local ownerLabel = ownerPlayer and ownerPlayer.Name or "Country-owned"
		print("Registered NPC:", npcModel.Name, "| Role:", role, "| Owner:", ownerLabel)
	end
end

-- Unregister an NPC from the combat system.
-- Cleanup order is mandatory:
--   Step 1: fetch npcRuntime
--   Step 2: call maid:DoCleaning() BEFORE clearing tables (callbacks may read context)
--   Step 3: nil npcRuntime entry
--   Step 4: clear all cross-NPC target/threat references
--   Step 5: nil all per-NPC combat state tables
-- Idempotent: second call on already-unregistered NPC is safe.
function Combat.unregisterNPC(npcModel)
	if not npcModel then return end

	-- FIX: Early-exit if this NPC was already unregistered (prevents redundant
	-- O(N) scans across all target/threat tables on the second call from
	-- the Died→Destroying double-fire path).
	if not npcRuntime[npcModel] and not npcOwners[npcModel] then
		return
	end

	cleanupDebugParts(npcModel.Name)

	-- Step 1: fetch runtime state
	local runtime = npcRuntime[npcModel]

	-- Step 2: clean maid before clearing tables so any callbacks in DoCleaning can still read state
	if runtime then
		runtime.maid:DoCleaning()
	end

	-- Step 3: nil the runtime entry
	npcRuntime[npcModel] = nil

	-- Step 4: Remove this NPC from all other NPCs' target/threat lists
	for otherNPC, targets in pairs(manualTargets) do
		for i = #targets, 1, -1 do
			if targets[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(targets, i)
			end
		end
	end

	for defender, attackers in pairs(defenderAttackers) do
		for i = #attackers, 1, -1 do
			if attackers[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(attackers, i)
			end
		end
	end

	for attacker, threats in pairs(attackerThreats) do
		for i = #threats, 1, -1 do
			if threats[i] == npcModel then
				table.remove(threats, i)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Step 5: clear all per-NPC combat state tables
	manualTargets[npcModel] = nil
	npcOwners[npcModel] = nil
	npcRoles[npcModel] = nil
	npcCooldown[npcModel] = nil
	defenderAttackers[npcModel] = nil
	attackerThreats[npcModel] = nil
	pathTimestamps[npcModel] = nil
	combatLoops[npcModel] = nil
	npcInCombat[npcModel] = nil
end

-- Track when an attacker is targeting a defender (for defender auto-retaliation)
function Combat.noteAttackerTargeting(attackerModel, defenderModel)
	if not attackerModel or not defenderModel then return end
	if not defenderAttackers[defenderModel] then
		defenderAttackers[defenderModel] = {}
	end

	local found = false
	for _, v in ipairs(defenderAttackers[defenderModel]) do
		if v == attackerModel then found = true break end
	end

	if not found then
		table.insert(defenderAttackers[defenderModel], attackerModel)
		if DEBUG then
			print("[Combat] Defender " .. defenderModel.Name .. " now tracking " .. #defenderAttackers[defenderModel] .. " attacker(s)")
		end
	end
end

-- Track when someone is targeting an attacker (for attacker auto-retaliation)
function Combat.noteTargetingAttacker(aggressorModel, victimAttackerModel)
	if not aggressorModel or not victimAttackerModel then return end
	if not attackerThreats[victimAttackerModel] then
		attackerThreats[victimAttackerModel] = {}
	end

	local found = false
	for _, v in ipairs(attackerThreats[victimAttackerModel]) do
		if v == aggressorModel then found = true break end
	end

	if not found then
		table.insert(attackerThreats[victimAttackerModel], aggressorModel)
		if DEBUG then
			print("[Combat] Attacker " .. victimAttackerModel.Name .. " now tracking " .. #attackerThreats[victimAttackerModel] .. " threat(s)")
		end
	end
end

-- Record that attackerNpc hit targetNpc.
-- Disengage logic applies to ALL AttackerNPCs (player-owned and country-owned).
-- Auto-retaliation (threat tracking) only applies to NPCs with AutoRetaliate=true.
function Combat.noteHit(attackerNpc, targetNpc)
	if not attackerNpc or not targetNpc then return end
	if targetNpc:GetAttribute("Dead") then return end

	local targetRole = npcRoles[targetNpc]

	-- When any AttackerNPC is hit by an enemy that it is NOT already
	-- manually targeting, it disengages from all current manual targets
	-- so it stops its offensive. This applies to ALL AttackerNPCs.
	-- Only manualTargets is checked (not attackerThreats), because threats
	-- are registered early via handleSecondClick before combat even starts.
	if targetRole == "Attacker" then
		local alreadyTargeting = false

		local targets = manualTargets[targetNpc]
		if targets then
			for _, t in ipairs(targets) do
				if t == attackerNpc then
					alreadyTargeting = true
					break
				end
			end
		end

		if not alreadyTargeting then
			Combat.clearAllManualTargets(targetNpc)
			if DEBUG then
				print("[Combat] " .. targetNpc.Name .. " disengaged from manual targets after being attacked by " .. attackerNpc.Name)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Auto-retaliation threat tracking only for AutoRetaliate NPCs (country-owned)
	if targetNpc:GetAttribute("AutoRetaliate") ~= true then return end

	if targetRole == "Defender" then
		Combat.noteAttackerTargeting(attackerNpc, targetNpc)
	elseif targetRole == "Attacker" then
		Combat.noteTargetingAttacker(attackerNpc, targetNpc)
	end
end

function Combat.removeAttackerFromDefender(attackerModel, defenderModel)
	if not attackerModel or not defenderModel then return end
	local attackers = defenderAttackers[defenderModel]
	if not attackers then return end

	for i, att in ipairs(attackers) do
		if att == attackerModel then
			table.remove(attackers, i)
			if DEBUG then
				print("[Combat] " .. attackerModel.Name .. " removed from " .. defenderModel.Name .. "'s threat list")
			end
			break
		end
	end
end

-- Remove a threat from an attacker's threat list
function Combat.removeThreatFromAttacker(threatModel, attackerModel)
	if not threatModel or not attackerModel then return end
	local threats = attackerThreats[attackerModel]
	if not threats then return end

	for i, threat in ipairs(threats) do
		if threat == threatModel then
			table.remove(threats, i)
			if DEBUG then
				print("[Combat] " .. threatModel.Name .. " removed from " .. attackerModel.Name .. "'s threat list")
			end
			break
		end
	end
end

function Combat.attackAttacker(attackerModel, targetAttackerModel)
	if not attackerModel or not targetAttackerModel then return end
	if not npcOwners[attackerModel] then return end

	-- Use country-based check so country-owned (nil-owner) NPCs are handled correctly
	if not DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(attackerModel, targetAttackerModel) then
		return -- Can't attack (same country, allied, or not at war)
	end

	Combat.addManualTarget(attackerModel, targetAttackerModel)
end

-- Helpers
function Combat.getOwner(npc) return npcOwners[npc] end
function Combat.getRole(npc) return npcRoles[npc] end
function Combat.isLoopRunning(npc) return combatLoops[npc] ~= nil end

-- Returns true when the NPC currently has active combat targets or is being attacked.
-- Used by NPCMovementSystem and NPCTargetingHandler to block/gate movement.
function Combat.isInCombat(npc)
	return npcInCombat[npc] == true
end

function Combat.getAttackerCount(defenderModel)
	local attackers = defenderAttackers[defenderModel]
	return attackers and #attackers or 0
end

-- Get threat count for an attacker
function Combat.getThreatCount(attackerModel)
	local threats = attackerThreats[attackerModel]
	return threats and #threats or 0
end

return Combat

--- src/shared/TileOwnershipManager.luau ---
-- TileOwnershipManager (ModuleScript in ServerScriptService)
-- Occupation stored by COUNTRY (not player) - persists when players leave
-- Capital capture guard + conquered state check
-- Single no-yield atomic ownership mutation path via state applicators

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")

local TileOwnershipManager = {}

-- Lazy-load dependencies
local ServerState = nil
local TileManager = nil
local TileAdjacencyManager = nil
local Combat = nil
local DiplomacyManager = nil
local CountryNPCRegistry = nil

local function getDependencies()
	if not ServerState then
		ServerState = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("ServerState", 10))
	end
	if not TileManager then
		TileManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileManager", 10))
	end
	if not TileAdjacencyManager then
		TileAdjacencyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileAdjacencyManager", 10))
	end
	if not Combat then
		Combat = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("NPCCombatSystem", 10))
	end
	if not DiplomacyManager then
		DiplomacyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("DiplomacyManager", 10))
	end
	if not CountryNPCRegistry then
		CountryNPCRegistry = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("CountryNPCRegistry", 10))
	end
end

-- Configuration
local DEBUG = false
local EUROPE_MAP = Workspace:WaitForChild("EuropeMap", 10)

-- Store original tile colors
local OriginalColors = {}

-- Track occupied territories by COUNTRY name (persists when player leaves)
-- OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] = { occupyingCountry = "France", originalCountry = "Germany", originalColor = Color3 }
local OccupiedTerritories = {}

-- Store country colors
local CountryColors = {}

-- Capital capture guard
local capitalsBeingCaptured = {}

---------------------------------------------------
-- Initialization
---------------------------------------------------

local function scanCountryColors()
	for _, countryModel in ipairs(EUROPE_MAP:GetChildren()) do
		if countryModel:IsA("Model") then
			local countryName = countryModel.Name

			for _, part in ipairs(countryModel:GetDescendants()) do
				if part:IsA("BasePart") then
					CountryColors[countryName] = part.Color
					OriginalColors[part] = part.Color
					break
				end
			end

			for _, part in ipairs(countryModel:GetDescendants()) do
				if part:IsA("BasePart") then
					OriginalColors[part] = part.Color
				end
			end
		end
	end

	if DEBUG then print("[TileOwnershipManager] Scanned country colors") end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Private: Color Resolution
---------------------------------------------------

-- Resolves the display color for a country.
-- Checks CountryColors cache first, then falls back to sampling OriginalColors
-- from the country's map Model. Caches the result on success.
local function resolveCountryColor(countryName)
	local color = CountryColors[countryName]
	if color then return color end

	-- Fallback: sample from direct children of country model
	local countryModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
	if countryModel then
		for _, child in ipairs(countryModel:GetChildren()) do
			if child:IsA("BasePart") and OriginalColors[child] then
				color = OriginalColors[child]
				CountryColors[countryName] = color
				return color
			end
		end
	end

	warn("[TileOwnership] resolveCountryColor: no color found for '" .. tostring(countryName) .. "'")
	return nil
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Private: Low-Level State Helpers
-- These are NOT public entry points — they are atomic building blocks only.
-- Every write to visual, logical, and occupied state flows through exactly one
-- of the three high-level applicators below, which call these helpers together
-- with no yield between them.
---------------------------------------------------

-- Set tile color to the controlling country's color.
-- Returns true on success, false if color could not be resolved (logs a warning).
local function applyTileVisualOwner(tilePart, ownerCountryName)
	local color = resolveCountryColor(ownerCountryName)
	if not color then
		warn("[TileOwnership] applyTileVisualOwner: no color for '" .. tostring(ownerCountryName) .. "' on tile " .. tilePart.Name)
		return false
	end
	tilePart.Color = color
	return true
end

-- Restore the tile to its original (pre-capture) visual state.
local function applyTileOriginalVisual(tilePart, originalColor)
	if not originalColor then
		warn("[TileOwnership] applyTileOriginalVisual: originalColor is nil for tile " .. tilePart.Name)
		return
	end
	tilePart.Color = originalColor
end

-- Set or clear the OwnerCountry attribute.
-- Pass a non-empty string to assign; pass nil or "" to clear.
local function setTileLogicalOwner(tilePart, ownerCountryNameOrNil)
	if type(ownerCountryNameOrNil) == "string" and ownerCountryNameOrNil ~= "" then
		tilePart:SetAttribute("OwnerCountry", ownerCountryNameOrNil)
	else
		tilePart:SetAttribute("OwnerCountry", nil)
	end
end

-- Write the OccupiedTerritories record for a tile.
local function setOccupiedRecord(tilePart, occupyingCountry, originalCountry, originalColor)
	OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] = {
		occupyingCountry = occupyingCountry,
		originalCountry = originalCountry,
		originalColor = originalColor,
	}
end

-- Delete the OccupiedTerritories record for a tile.
local function clearOccupiedRecord(tilePart)
	OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] = nil
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Private: High-Level State Applicators
-- These are the ONLY valid paths for changing tile ownership state.
-- All three writes (visual, logical, occupied record) happen synchronously
-- with no yield between them — this is the "atomic" guarantee.
---------------------------------------------------

-- Invariant A: Occupied but not annexed.
-- After this call:
--   OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] ~= nil
--   OwnerCountry == occupyingCountry
--   tilePart.Color == CountryColors[occupyingCountry]
-- Returns false if the occupying country has no resolvable color (no state written).
local function applyOccupiedState(tilePart, occupyingCountry, originalCountry, originalColor)
	if not applyTileVisualOwner(tilePart, occupyingCountry) then return false end
	setTileLogicalOwner(tilePart, occupyingCountry)
	setOccupiedRecord(tilePart, occupyingCountry, originalCountry, originalColor)
	return true
end

-- Invariant B: Annexed.
-- After this call:
--   OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] == nil
--   OwnerCountry == annexingCountry
--   tilePart.Color == CountryColors[annexingCountry]  (same color, tile was already colored for occupier)
-- Returns false if the annexing country has no resolvable color (no state written).
local function applyAnnexedState(tilePart, annexingCountry)
	if not applyTileVisualOwner(tilePart, annexingCountry) then return false end
	setTileLogicalOwner(tilePart, annexingCountry)
	clearOccupiedRecord(tilePart)
	return true
end

-- Invariant C/D: Reverted to geographic/original ownership.
-- After this call:
--   OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] == nil
--   OwnerCountry == nil
--   tilePart.Color == originalColor
local function applyOriginalState(tilePart, originalColor)
	applyTileOriginalVisual(tilePart, originalColor)
	setTileLogicalOwner(tilePart, nil)
	clearOccupiedRecord(tilePart)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Color Management
---------------------------------------------------

function TileOwnershipManager.getCountryColor(countryName)
	return CountryColors[countryName]
end

function TileOwnershipManager.getPlayerColor(player)
	getDependencies()
	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if playerCountry then
		return CountryColors[playerCountry]
	end
	return nil
end

function TileOwnershipManager.getOriginalColor(tilePart)
	return OriginalColors[tilePart]
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Country-based Occupation System
---------------------------------------------------

-- Check if a tile is occupied by a specific COUNTRY
function TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedByCountry(tilePart, countryName)
	local data = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	return data and data.occupyingCountry == countryName
end

-- Check if a tile is occupied by a specific PLAYER's country
function TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedBy(tilePart, player)
	getDependencies()
	if not player then return false end

	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not playerCountry then return false end

	return TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedByCountry(tilePart, playerCountry)
end

-- Check if a tile is occupied by anyone
function TileOwnershipManager.isOccupied(tilePart)
	return OccupiedTerritories[tilePart] ~= nil
end

-- Get which COUNTRY occupies a tile
function TileOwnershipManager.getOccupyingCountry(tilePart)
	local data = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	return data and data.occupyingCountry
end

-- Get the original country of an occupied tile
function TileOwnershipManager.getOriginalCountry(tilePart)
	getDependencies()
	local data = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	if data then
		return data.originalCountry
	end
	return TileAdjacencyManager.getTileCountry(tilePart)
end

-- Check if tile belongs to a country (own territory OR occupied by them)
function TileOwnershipManager.tileEffectivelyBelongsTo(tilePart, countryName)
	getDependencies()

	if not tilePart or not countryName then return false end

	-- Check explicit ownership attribute first (set on capture and annexation)
	-- This handles annexed tiles that stay in their original country Model
	local ownerAttr = tilePart:GetAttribute("OwnerCountry")
	if ownerAttr then
		return ownerAttr == countryName
	end

	-- Check if it's their home territory (no ownership attribute = never captured)
	local tileCountry = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileCountry(tilePart)
	if tileCountry == countryName then
		return true
	end

	-- Check if they've occupied it
	return TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedByCountry(tilePart, countryName)
end

-- Check if tile belongs to player's country
function TileOwnershipManager.tileBelongsToPlayer(tilePart, player)
	getDependencies()
	if not player then return false end

	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not playerCountry then return false end

	return TileOwnershipManager.tileEffectivelyBelongsTo(tilePart, playerCountry)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Public Mutation Functions
-- All tile state changes flow through the state applicators above.
---------------------------------------------------

-- Capture a tile (store by country, not player)
function TileOwnershipManager.captureTile(tilePart, player)
	getDependencies()

	if not tilePart or not player then return false end

	local geographicCountry = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileCountry(tilePart)
	local effectiveOwner = TileAdjacencyManager.getEffectiveOwner(tilePart)
	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)

	if not playerCountry then
		warn("[TileOwnership] Player has no country")
		return false
	end

	-- Don't capture tiles already effectively owned by you
	if effectiveOwner == playerCountry then
		return false
	end

	-- RECLAIM: Tile is geographically ours but controlled by someone else (annexed).
	-- Restore to original geographic state (Invariant D).
	-- Must come BEFORE isOccupiedByCountry to avoid early-return on residual entries.
	if geographicCountry == playerCountry then
		local origColor = OriginalColors[tilePart]
		if not origColor then
			warn("[TileOwnership] captureTile reclaim: no original color for tile " .. tilePart.Name)
			return false
		end

		-- Invariant D: reclaimed original land relies on geography again.
		-- OwnerCountry = nil, no occupied record, original color restored.
		applyOriginalState(tilePart, origColor)

		if DEBUG then
			print("[TileOwnership] " .. playerCountry .. " reclaimed annexed tile (was owned by " .. tostring(effectiveOwner) .. ")")
		end

		-- Fire event AFTER all state writes are complete
		local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")
		if TileCapturedEvent then
			TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, player.Name, playerCountry)
		end
		return true
	end

	-- Don't re-capture already occupied tiles by same country
	if TileOwnershipManager.isOccupiedByCountry(tilePart, playerCountry) then
		return false
	end

	-- Preserve original data if tile is already occupied by another country.
	-- This ensures peace treaties revert to the true original owner's color.
	local existingOccupation = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	local storedOriginalCountry, storedOriginalColor

	if existingOccupation then
		storedOriginalCountry = existingOccupation.originalCountry
		storedOriginalColor = existingOccupation.originalColor
	else
		storedOriginalCountry = geographicCountry
		storedOriginalColor = OriginalColors[tilePart] or tilePart.Color
	end

	-- Invariant A: occupied state — all three writes happen together, no yield.
	if not applyOccupiedState(tilePart, playerCountry, storedOriginalCountry, storedOriginalColor) then
		-- applyOccupiedState already warned about missing color
		return false
	end

	if DEBUG then
		print("[TileOwnership] " .. playerCountry .. " captured tile in " .. (geographicCountry or "unknown"))
	end

	-- Fire event AFTER all state writes are complete
	local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")
	if TileCapturedEvent then
		TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, player.Name, playerCountry)
	end

	return true
end

-- Release a captured tile (revert to geographic/original state)
function TileOwnershipManager.releaseTile(tilePart)
	local data = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	if not data then return false end

	local originalCountry = data.originalCountry
	local originalColor = data.originalColor

	-- Invariant C: reverted to geographic owner — all three writes together, no yield.
	applyOriginalState(tilePart, originalColor)

	if DEBUG then
		print("[TileOwnership] Released tile back to " .. (originalCountry or "unknown"))
	end

	-- Fire event AFTER all state writes are complete.
	-- Notify clients so they cancel any in-flight tween and start one to the correct color.
	local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")
	if TileCapturedEvent and originalCountry then
		TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, "", originalCountry)
	end

	return true
end

-- Reclaim a tile that was occupied by an enemy back to its original owner.
-- BUG FIX: Previous version omitted the OwnerCountry clear, leaving the attribute stale.
function TileOwnershipManager.reclaimTile(tilePart, player)
	getDependencies()

	if not tilePart or not player then return false end

	local data = OccupiedTerritories[tilePart]
	if not data then return false end

	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not playerCountry then return false end

	-- Only reclaim if the tile's original country matches the player's country
	if data.originalCountry ~= playerCountry then
		return false
	end

	local occupyingCountry = data.occupyingCountry
	local originalColor = data.originalColor

	-- Invariant D: reclaimed original land relies on geography again.
	-- BUG FIX: now explicitly clears OwnerCountry (was missing before).
	-- OwnerCountry = nil, no occupied record, original color restored.
	applyOriginalState(tilePart, originalColor)

	if DEBUG then
		print("[TileOwnership] " .. playerCountry .. " reclaimed tile from " .. occupyingCountry)
	end

	-- Fire tile captured event AFTER all state writes are complete
	local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")
	if TileCapturedEvent then
		TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, player.Name, playerCountry)
	end

	return true
end

-- Release all tiles occupied by a specific COUNTRY (used in peace treaties).
-- BUG FIX: Previous version omitted the OwnerCountry clear on each released tile.
function TileOwnershipManager.releaseCountryOccupiedTiles(countryName)
	local releasedCount = 0

	-- FIX: Collect keys first to avoid modifying table during pairs() iteration
	local tilesToRelease = {}
	for tilePart, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
		if data.occupyingCountry == countryName then
			table.insert(tilesToRelease, { tilePart = tilePart, data = data })
		end
	end

	local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")

	for _, entry in ipairs(tilesToRelease) do
		local tilePart = entry.tilePart
		local data = entry.data

		if tilePart and tilePart.Parent then
			-- Invariant C: all three writes together, no yield.
			-- BUG FIX: now explicitly clears OwnerCountry (was missing before).
			applyOriginalState(tilePart, data.originalColor)
			-- Fire event AFTER state is fully applied
			if TileCapturedEvent and data.originalCountry then
				TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, "", data.originalCountry)
			end
		else
			-- Part was destroyed — clear the orphaned record to prevent memory leak
			clearOccupiedRecord(tilePart)
		end
		releasedCount = releasedCount + 1
	end

	if DEBUG and releasedCount > 0 then
		print("[TileOwnership] Released " .. releasedCount .. " tiles from " .. countryName)
	end

	return releasedCount
end

-- Get all tiles occupied by a specific COUNTRY
function TileOwnershipManager.getCountryOccupiedTiles(countryName)
	local tiles = {}
	for tilePart, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
		if data.occupyingCountry == countryName then
			table.insert(tiles, tilePart)
		end
	end
	return tiles
end

-- Get count of tiles occupied by a country
function TileOwnershipManager.getCountryOccupiedCount(countryName)
	local count = 0
	for _, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
		if data.occupyingCountry == countryName then
			count = count + 1
		end
	end
	return count
end

-- Annex occupied tiles: convert occupied territory to core territory.
-- Used when signing peace — occupied tiles become permanent part of the occupying country.
function TileOwnershipManager.annexOccupiedTiles(countryName)
	local annexedCount = 0

	-- Collect tiles to annex
	local tilesToAnnex = {}
	for tilePart, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
		if data.occupyingCountry == countryName then
			table.insert(tilesToAnnex, { tile = tilePart, data = data })
		end
	end

	local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")

	for _, entry in ipairs(tilesToAnnex) do
		local tilePart = entry.tile

		if tilePart and tilePart.Parent then
			-- Invariant B: annexed — no occupied record, OwnerCountry set, color re-confirmed.
			-- applyAnnexedState re-resolves the color (same as occupying color, effectively no-op visually).
			if applyAnnexedState(tilePart, countryName) then
				annexedCount = annexedCount + 1
				-- Fire event AFTER all state writes are complete
				if TileCapturedEvent then
					TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(tilePart, "", countryName)
				end
			end
		end
	end

	if DEBUG and annexedCount > 0 then
		print("[TileOwnership] Annexed " .. annexedCount .. " tiles to " .. countryName)
	end

	return annexedCount
end

-- Legacy: Get tiles occupied by player (uses their country)
function TileOwnershipManager.getPlayerOccupiedTiles(player)
	getDependencies()
	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not playerCountry then return {} end
	return TileOwnershipManager.getCountryOccupiedTiles(playerCountry)
end

-- Legacy: Get count for player
function TileOwnershipManager.getOccupiedTileCount(player)
	getDependencies()
	local playerCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not playerCountry then return 0 end
	return TileOwnershipManager.getCountryOccupiedCount(playerCountry)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Capital Capture & Country Takeover
---------------------------------------------------

function TileOwnershipManager.isCapitalBeingCaptured(countryName)
	return capitalsBeingCaptured[countryName] == true
end

function TileOwnershipManager.captureCapital(losingCountryName, winningPlayer)
	getDependencies()

	if not losingCountryName or not winningPlayer then return false end

	if capitalsBeingCaptured[losingCountryName] then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[TileOwnership] Capital capture already in progress for " .. losingCountryName)
		end
		return false
	end

	-- Check if the country is already conquered
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	local currentOwner = CountryOwners[losingCountryName]
	if type(currentOwner) == "string" and currentOwner:find("Conquered_") then
		if DEBUG then
			print("[TileOwnership] Cannot capture " .. losingCountryName .. " - already conquered by " .. currentOwner)
		end
		return false
	end

	capitalsBeingCaptured[losingCountryName] = true

	local losingPlayer = currentOwner
	local winningCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(winningPlayer)

	if DEBUG then print("[TileOwnership] CAPITAL CAPTURED! " .. winningPlayer.Name .. " (" .. winningCountry .. ") conquered " .. losingCountryName) end

	local GlobalNotificationEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GlobalNotificationEvent")
	if GlobalNotificationEvent then
		local msg = "👑 CONQUEST! " .. winningCountry .. " has conquered " .. losingCountryName .. "!"
		GlobalNotificationEvent:FireAllClients(msg, Color3.fromRGB(255, 215, 0))
	end

	TileOwnershipManager.performCountryTakeover(losingCountryName, winningPlayer, losingPlayer)

	-- Clear the guard after takeover is fully complete (not on a timer)
	capitalsBeingCaptured[losingCountryName] = nil

	return true
end

function TileOwnershipManager.performCountryTakeover(losingCountryName, winningPlayer, losingPlayer)
	getDependencies()

	local winningCountry = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(winningPlayer)

	-- Batched tile capture list — fire ONE RemoteEvent at the end instead of per-tile
	local capturedTilesBatch = {}

	-- 1. TRANSFER TILES in the loser's own country model.
	-- Uses cached TileParts from TileAdjacencyManager instead of expensive GetDescendants().
	-- For each tile: decide final ownership state, then apply visual + attribute + record together.
	local loserTileParts = TileAdjacencyManager.getCountryTileParts(losingCountryName)
	for _, part in ipairs(loserTileParts) do
		-- Mark conquered capital tiles with attributes (defense-in-depth)
		if part.Name == "Capital" then
			part:SetAttribute("FormerCapitalOf", losingCountryName)
			part:SetAttribute("ConqueredBy", winningCountry)
		end

		local occupationData = OccupiedTerritories[part]
		if occupationData then
			if occupationData.occupyingCountry ~= winningCountry
				and occupationData.occupyingCountry ~= losingCountryName then
				-- Third party occupies this tile — leave their color and ownership intact
				if DEBUG then
					print(string.format("[TileOwnership] Skipping %s (third-party: %s)",
						part.Name, occupationData.occupyingCountry))
				end
			else
				-- Loser or winner had it — transfer to winner (Invariant A: occupied state)
				if applyOccupiedState(part, winningCountry, occupationData.originalCountry, occupationData.originalColor) then
					table.insert(capturedTilesBatch, part)
				end
			end
		else
			-- Unoccupied core territory — winner takes it (Invariant A: occupied state).
			-- Capture origColor BEFORE applyOccupiedState changes part.Color.
			local origColor = OriginalColors[part] or part.Color
			if applyOccupiedState(part, winningCountry, losingCountryName, origColor) then
				table.insert(capturedTilesBatch, part)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Third-party occupied tiles remain with their current occupier.
	if DEBUG then
		local thirdPartyCount = 0
		for _, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
			if data.originalCountry == losingCountryName and data.occupyingCountry ~= winningCountry then
				thirdPartyCount = thirdPartyCount + 1
			end
		end
		if thirdPartyCount > 0 then
			print(string.format("[TileOwnership] %d tiles in %s remain with third-party occupiers (not transferred to %s)",
				thirdPartyCount, losingCountryName, winningCountry))
		end
	end

	-- Recover orphaned tiles from countries the loser had previously conquered
	-- (Previous conquests may have lost their OccupiedTerritories entries)
	local CountryOwnersSnapshot = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	local function collectConqueredCountries(countryName, collected)
		collected = collected or {}
		for cName, owner in pairs(CountryOwnersSnapshot) do
			if type(owner) == "string" and owner == "Conquered_" .. countryName then
				if not collected[cName] then
					collected[cName] = true
					collectConqueredCountries(cName, collected)
				end
			end
		end
		return collected
	end

	local conqueredByLoser = collectConqueredCountries(losingCountryName)
	for conqueredName, _ in pairs(conqueredByLoser) do
		-- Use cached tile parts instead of GetDescendants()
		local conqueredTileParts = TileAdjacencyManager.getCountryTileParts(conqueredName)
		for _, part in ipairs(conqueredTileParts) do
			if OriginalColors[part] then
				local existingData = OccupiedTerritories[part]
				if not existingData then
					-- Orphaned tile — winner claims it (Invariant A)
					if applyOccupiedState(part, winningCountry, conqueredName, OriginalColors[part]) then
						table.insert(capturedTilesBatch, part)
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end

	-- FIX (Bug 2): Transfer ownership of ALL occupied territories belonging to the loser
	-- (tiles in other countries' models that the loser was occupying).
	-- Collect BEFORE mutating OccupiedTerritories to avoid iteration issues.
	local tilesToTransfer = {}
	for tilePart, data in pairs(OccupiedTerritories) do
		if data.occupyingCountry == losingCountryName then
			table.insert(tilesToTransfer, { tilePart = tilePart, data = data })
		end
	end

	for _, entry in ipairs(tilesToTransfer) do
		local tilePart = entry.tilePart
		local data = entry.data

		if tilePart and tilePart.Parent then
			-- Transfer to winner (Invariant A: occupied state)
			if applyOccupiedState(tilePart, winningCountry, data.originalCountry, data.originalColor) then
				table.insert(capturedTilesBatch, tilePart)
			end

			if DEBUG then
				print(string.format("[TileOwnership] Annexed %s's occupied tile from %s to %s (tile stays in %s's Model)",
					losingCountryName, data.originalCountry, winningCountry, data.originalCountry))
			end
		end
	end

	-- Fire ONE batched RemoteEvent for all captured tiles instead of per-tile spam
	if #capturedTilesBatch > 0 then
		local TileCapturedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("TileCapturedEvent")
		if TileCapturedEvent then
