			TileCapturedEvent:FireAllClients(capturedTilesBatch, winningPlayer.Name, winningCountry)
		end
	end

	-- Do NOT call releaseCountryOccupiedTiles() — that's for peace treaties, not conquests

	-- 2. TRANSFER RESOURCES
	if losingPlayer and typeof(losingPlayer) == "Instance" and losingPlayer:IsA("Player") and losingPlayer.Parent then
		local loserStats = losingPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
		local winnerStats = winningPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")

		-- FIX: Added proper nil checks for loserStats and winnerStats
		if loserStats and winnerStats then
			local loserCoins = loserStats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
			local winnerCoins = winnerStats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
			if loserCoins and winnerCoins then
				winnerCoins.Value = winnerCoins.Value + loserCoins.Value
				loserCoins.Value = 0
			end

			local loserManpower = loserStats:FindFirstChild("Manpower")
			local winnerManpower = winnerStats:FindFirstChild("Manpower")
			if loserManpower and winnerManpower then
				winnerManpower.Value = winnerManpower.Value + loserManpower.Value
				loserManpower.Value = 0
			end
		elseif DEBUG then
			warn("[TileOwnership] Could not transfer resources - leaderstats missing")
		end
	else
		-- Country was unowned — transfer from ServerState
		local countryCoins = ServerState.getCountryCoins(losingCountryName)
		local countryManpower = ServerState.getCountryManpower(losingCountryName)

		local winnerStats = winningPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
		if winnerStats then
			local winnerCoins = winnerStats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
			local winnerManpower = winnerStats:FindFirstChild("Manpower")

			if winnerCoins then
				winnerCoins.Value = winnerCoins.Value + countryCoins
			end
			if winnerManpower then
				winnerManpower.Value = winnerManpower.Value + countryManpower
			end
		end

		ServerState.setCountryCoins(losingCountryName, 0)
		ServerState.setCountryManpower(losingCountryName, 0)
	end

	-- 3. DESTROY conquered country's NPCs (winner inherits income, not units)
	local npcsToDestroy = CountryNPCRegistry.getNPCs(losingCountryName)
	for _, npc in ipairs(npcsToDestroy) do
		local humanoid = npc:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if humanoid then
			humanoid.Health = 0 -- triggers existing NPCSpawner cleanup pipeline
		end
	end
	if DEBUG then
		print("[TileOwnership] Destroyed " .. #npcsToDestroy .. " NPCs from conquered " .. losingCountryName)
	end

	-- 4. UPDATE COUNTRY OWNERSHIP
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	CountryOwners[losingCountryName] = "Conquered_" .. winningCountry
	ServerState.setCountryOwners(CountryOwners)

	-- Clear all diplomacy (wars, alliances, NAPs) involving the conquered country
	DiplomacyManager.clearAllDiplomacyForCountry(losingCountryName)

	-- 5. HANDLE LOSING PLAYER
	if losingPlayer and typeof(losingPlayer) == "Instance" and losingPlayer:IsA("Player") and losingPlayer.Parent then
		local loserStats = losingPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
		if loserStats then
			local countryStat = loserStats:FindFirstChild("Country")
			if countryStat then
				-- Use "None" (not "Defeated") so the client CountrySelectionScreen
				-- re-opens on the next CharacterAdded. The defeat notification is
				-- already sent via GlobalNotificationEvent above.
				countryStat.Value = "None"
			end
		end

		if losingPlayer.Character then
			local humanoid = losingPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if humanoid then
				humanoid.Health = 0
			end
		end

		local GlobalNotificationEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GlobalNotificationEvent")
		if GlobalNotificationEvent then
			GlobalNotificationEvent:FireClient(losingPlayer, "💀 Your capital has fallen! You have been defeated.", Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0))
		end

		TileManager.updatePlayerCountryCache(losingPlayer, nil)
	end

	-- DEBUG: Sanity check — detect tiles that should be owned but are missing OccupiedTerritories
	if DEBUG then
		local missingCount = 0
		local allCountriesToCheck = { losingCountryName }
		for cName, _ in pairs(conqueredByLoser) do
			table.insert(allCountriesToCheck, cName)
		end
		for _, cName in ipairs(allCountriesToCheck) do
			local cModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(cName)
			if cModel then
				for _, part in ipairs(cModel:GetDescendants()) do
					if part:IsA("BasePart") and OriginalColors[part] then
						if not OccupiedTerritories[part] then
							missingCount = missingCount + 1
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
		if missingCount > 0 then
			warn(string.format("[TileOwnership] SANITY CHECK FAILED: %d tiles missing OccupiedTerritories after takeover of %s",
				missingCount, losingCountryName))
		end
	end

	if DEBUG then print("[TileOwnership] Country takeover complete: " .. losingCountryName .. " -> " .. winningCountry) end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Initialize
---------------------------------------------------

scanCountryColors()

-- Do NOT auto-release on player leave - territories persist!

if DEBUG then print("[TileOwnershipManager] Initialization complete") end

return TileOwnershipManager

--- src/server/CountryManager.server.luau ---
-- CountryManager (ServerScriptService)
-- Wars and occupied territory persist when player leaves
-- New player inherits wars and occupied tiles

local DEBUG = false

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Core Data
local CountryOwners = {}

-- Track initialization state
local isInitialized = false

-- Forward-declare modules (assigned after require below)
local TileManager = nil

---------------------------------------------------
-- EARLY SETUP: Register OnServerInvoke BEFORE heavy module requires.
-- If a client calls InvokeServer() before this handler exists, Roblox
-- hangs the call indefinitely — which is the root cause of the intermittent
-- black/missing country-selection screen.
---------------------------------------------------
local GetAvailableCountries = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("GetAvailableCountries", 10)
if GetAvailableCountries then
	GetAvailableCountries.OnServerInvoke = function(requestingPlayer)
		if not isInitialized or not TileManager then
			return nil -- nil = server not ready; client should retry
		end

		-- Server-authoritative ownership check: if the player already owns a
		-- country, return false so the client knows to hide the selection screen
		-- instead of relying on the replicated Country stat (which can be stale
		-- due to replication delay after death/reset).
		for _, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
			if owner == requestingPlayer then
				return false
			end
		end

		local ok, result = pcall(TileManager.getAvailableCountries)
		if ok then
			return result
		else
			warn("[CountryManager] GetAvailableCountries crashed!")
			return nil
		end
	end
end

-- Configuration (heavy requires — these can yield for seconds while scanning tiles)
local EUROPE_MAP = Workspace:WaitForChild("EuropeMap", 10)
local COUNTRY_SELECTION_GUI_NAME = "CountrySelectionScreen"
local ServerState = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("ServerState", 10))
TileManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileManager", 10))
-- DiplomacyManager NOT cleared when player leaves (wars persist)
local DiplomacyManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("DiplomacyManager", 10))
local NPCSpawner = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("NPCSpawner", 10))
local CountryNPCRegistry = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("CountryNPCRegistry", 10))
local CountryClaimedEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("CountryClaimedEvent")

-- Income Loop States (table so generic helper can index by string key)
local loopRunning = {
	CoinLoopRunning = false,
	ManpowerLoopRunning = false,
}

-- Income Configuration
local COIN_INTERVAL = 10
local BASE_COIN_INCOME = 50

local MANPOWER_INTERVAL = 3
local BASE_MANPOWER_INCOME = 100

-- Starting resource configuration
local STARTING_COINS = 250

-- Per-player claiming lock
local playerClaiming = {}
local playerClaimTime = {}

---------------------------------------------------
-- Manpower Calculation System
---------------------------------------------------

local function calculateStartingManpower(stats, globalMins, globalMaxes, weights)
	-- Normalization: Scales values to a 0.0 - 1.0 range
	local function normalize(value, minVal, maxVal)
		if maxVal <= minVal then return 0.5 end 
		return math.clamp((value - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal), 0, 1)
	end

	local normPop = normalize(stats.population, globalMins.population, globalMaxes.population)
	local normTiles = normalize(stats.tileCount, globalMins.tileCount, globalMaxes.tileCount)
	local normArea = normalize(stats.totalArea, globalMins.totalArea, globalMaxes.totalArea)

	-- Weighted score determines where the country sits on the 5k - 90k spectrum
	local finalScore = (normPop * weights.population) + 
					   (normTiles * weights.tileCount) + 
					   (normArea * weights.totalArea)

	local MIN_MANPOWER = 5000
	local MAX_MANPOWER = 90000

	return math.floor(MIN_MANPOWER + ((MAX_MANPOWER - MIN_MANPOWER) * finalScore))
end

local function calculateAllStartingManpower()
	local startingManpower = {}
	local finalStats = {}
	
	-- Pull physical stats already calculated by TileManager
	local physicalStats = TileManager.getAllCountryTileStats()
	
	local globalMins = { population = math.huge, tileCount = math.huge, totalArea = math.huge }
	local globalMaxes = { population = 0, tileCount = 0, totalArea = 0 }
	local countryCount = 0

	-- 1. Combine Physical Stats with Population Data
	for countryName, stats in pairs(physicalStats) do
		local countryModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
		if countryModel then
			local popValue = countryModel:FindFirstChild("Population")
			local population = popValue and popValue.Value or 20000 -- Fallback population

			finalStats[countryName] = {
				population = population,
				tileCount = stats.tileCount,
				totalArea = stats.totalArea
			}

			-- Update Global Extremes for normalization
			globalMins.population = math.min(globalMins.population, population)
			globalMaxes.population = math.max(globalMaxes.population, population)
			globalMins.tileCount = math.min(globalMins.tileCount, stats.tileCount)
			globalMaxes.tileCount = math.max(globalMaxes.tileCount, stats.tileCount)
			globalMins.totalArea = math.min(globalMins.totalArea, stats.totalArea)
			globalMaxes.totalArea = math.max(globalMaxes.totalArea, stats.totalArea)
			
			countryCount = countryCount + 1
		end
	end

	if countryCount == 0 then
		warn("[CountryManager] No stats found in TileManager! Manpower defaulted.")
		return startingManpower
	end

	-- 2. Define Weights
	local weights = {
		totalArea = 0.35,  -- 35% weight on physical landmass (Secondary)
		population = 0.50, -- 50% weight on population (Primary)
		tileCount = 0.15   -- 15% weight on administrative density (Modifier)
	}

	-- 3. Run final calculations
	for countryName, stats in pairs(finalStats) do
		local manpower = calculateStartingManpower(stats, globalMins, globalMaxes, weights)
		startingManpower[countryName] = manpower
		if DEBUG then
			print(string.format("[CountryManager] %s Manpower: %d (Pop: %d, Tiles: %d, Area: %.0f)",
				countryName, manpower, stats.population, stats.tileCount, stats.totalArea))
		end
	end

	return startingManpower
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Helper Functions
---------------------------------------------------

local function getCapitalCFrame(countryName)
	local countryModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
	if not countryModel then return nil end
	local capitalPart = countryModel:FindFirstChild("Capital")
	if not capitalPart then
		return countryModel:GetPivot() * CFrame.new(0,5,0)
	end
	return capitalPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, capitalPart.Size.Y/2 + 5, 0)
end

local function transferCountryNPCs(countryName, newOwner)
	local Combat = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("NPCCombatSystem", 10))
	local npcs = CountryNPCRegistry.getNPCs(countryName)

	for _, npc in ipairs(npcs) do
		local ownerValue = npc:FindFirstChild("NPCOwner")
		if ownerValue then
			ownerValue.Value = newOwner
		end

		if newOwner then
			local role = Combat.getRole(npc)
			if role then
				Combat.transferOwnership(npc, newOwner)
				if DEBUG then
					print("[CountryManager] Transferred " .. npc.Name .. " to " .. newOwner.Name)
				end
			end
		else
			Combat.transferOwnership(npc, nil)
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. npc.Name .. " now country-owned (no player)")
			end
		end
	end

	return #npcs
end

-- Release countries WITHOUT clearing diplomacy or occupied territories
local function releasePlayerCountries(player, reason)
	local releasedAny = false
	for country, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		if owner == player then
			releasedAny = true
			local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")

			-- Save coins to country (for next player)
			local coins = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
			if coins then
				ServerState.setCountryCoins(country, math.floor(coins.Value))
				if DEBUG then
					print("[CountryManager] Saved " .. coins.Value .. " coins to " .. country)
				end
				coins.Value = 0
			end

			-- Save manpower to country
			local manpower = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Manpower")
			if manpower then
				ServerState.setCountryManpower(country, math.floor(manpower.Value))
				if DEBUG then
					print("[CountryManager] Saved " .. manpower.Value .. " manpower to " .. country)
				end
				manpower.Value = 0
			end

			-- Transfer NPCs to country ownership (no player)
			local npcCount = transferCountryNPCs(country, nil)
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. country .. " now has " .. npcCount .. " NPCs waiting for next player")
			end

			-- Do NOT clear diplomacy - wars persist!
			-- DiplomacyManager.clearCountryDiplomacy(country) -- REMOVED

			-- Do NOT release occupied territories - they persist!
			-- Occupied territories remain owned by the COUNTRY

			-- Release the country (mark as Unowned but keep wars active)
			CountryOwners[country] = "Unowned"
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. country .. " released - " .. player.Name .. " " .. reason)
				print("[CountryManager] Wars and occupied territories for " .. country .. " remain active")
			end

			-- Clear TileManager cache for this player
			TileManager.updatePlayerCountryCache(player, nil)

			-- Reset leaderstats
			local countryStat = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Country")
			if countryStat then
				countryStat.Value = "None"
			end
		end
	end
	ServerState.setCountryOwners(CountryOwners)

	-- Hide BuyNPCGui for the released player (client will re-show selection screen via CharacterAdded)
	if releasedAny and player.Parent then
		local playerGui = player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		if playerGui then
			local buyGui = playerGui:FindFirstChild("BuyNPCGui")
			if buyGui then
				buyGui.Enabled = false
				local mainFrame = buyGui:FindFirstChild("MainFrame")
				if mainFrame then mainFrame.Visible = false end
			end
		end
	end
end

local function hasAnyOwnedCountries()
	for countryName, ownerValue in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		if typeof(ownerValue) == "Instance" and ownerValue:IsA("Player") then
			return true
		end
		if type(ownerValue) == "string" and ownerValue:sub(1, 10) == "Conquered_" then
			local resolved = ServerState.resolveCountryOwner(countryName)
			if resolved and typeof(resolved) == "Instance" and resolved:IsA("Player") and resolved.Parent then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	return false
end

-- Generic income loop helper (coin and manpower loops differ only in config)
local function startIncomeLoop(config)
	-- config.loopFlag: string key into loopRunning table
	-- config.interval: number (seconds between ticks)
	-- config.incomeAmount: number (amount added per tick)
	-- config.statName: string ("Coins" or "Manpower")
	-- config.statSetter: function(countryName, amount)
	local includeConqueredCountries = config.includeConqueredCountries ~= false
	while loopRunning[config.loopFlag] do
		if not hasAnyOwnedCountries() then
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] No owned countries remaining. Stopping " .. config.statName .. " income loop.")
			end
			loopRunning[config.loopFlag] = false
			break
		end

		local now = os.clock()

		for countryName, ownerValue in pairs(CountryOwners) do
			local resolvedOwner
			local isDirectlyOwned = false

			if typeof(ownerValue) == "Instance" and ownerValue:IsA("Player") then
				resolvedOwner = ownerValue
				isDirectlyOwned = true
			elseif includeConqueredCountries and type(ownerValue) == "string" and ownerValue:sub(1, 10) == "Conquered_" then
				resolvedOwner = ServerState.resolveCountryOwner(countryName)
			end

			if not resolvedOwner or typeof(resolvedOwner) ~= "Instance"
				or not resolvedOwner:IsA("Player") or not resolvedOwner.Parent then
				continue
			end

			local claimTime = playerClaimTime[resolvedOwner]
			if claimTime and (now - claimTime) < config.interval then
				continue
			end

			local leaderstats = resolvedOwner:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
			local statObj = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild(config.statName)

			if statObj then
				local newAmount = math.floor(statObj.Value) + config.incomeAmount
				statObj.Value = newAmount
				-- Only mirror to country treasury for directly-owned countries
				if isDirectlyOwned then
					config.statSetter(countryName, newAmount)
				end
			end
		end
		task.wait(config.interval)
	end
	if DEBUG then
		print("[CountryManager] " .. config.statName .. " income loop stopped.")
	end
end

-- Thin wrappers preserve original function names for callers
local function startCoinIncomeLoop()
	startIncomeLoop({
		loopFlag = "CoinLoopRunning",
		interval = COIN_INTERVAL,
		incomeAmount = BASE_COIN_INCOME,
		statName = "Coins",
		statSetter = ServerState.setCountryCoins,
	})
end

local function startManpowerIncomeLoop()
	startIncomeLoop({
		loopFlag = "ManpowerLoopRunning",
		interval = MANPOWER_INTERVAL,
		incomeAmount = BASE_MANPOWER_INCOME,
		statName = "Manpower",
		statSetter = ServerState.setCountryManpower,
		includeConqueredCountries = false,
	})
end

local function onCharacterRemoving(player, character)
	releasePlayerCountries(player, "died/reset")
end

local function handleCountrySelection(player, countryName)
	if not isInitialized then
		warn("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " tried to claim before initialization complete.")
		return
	end

	if playerClaiming[player] then
		warn("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " is already claiming a country.")
		return
	end
	playerClaiming[player] = true

	local claimSucceeded = false
	local claimedCountryName = nil

	local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
		-- Check if country is available (Unowned, not owned by another player)
		local currentOwner = CountryOwners[countryName]
		if currentOwner and currentOwner ~= "Unowned" then
			-- Check if it's a player
			if typeof(currentOwner) == "Instance" and currentOwner:IsA("Player") then
				error(player.Name .. " attempted to claim " .. countryName .. " but it is already owned by " .. currentOwner.Name)
				-- Check if conquered
			elseif type(currentOwner) == "string" and currentOwner:find("Conquered_") then
				error(player.Name .. " attempted to claim " .. countryName .. " but it has been conquered")
			end
		end

		for country, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
			if owner == player then
				error(player.Name .. " already owns " .. country .. ". Cannot claim another.")
			end
		end

		CountryOwners[countryName] = player
		ServerState.setCountryOwners(CountryOwners)
		claimedCountryName = countryName
		claimSucceeded = true
		if DEBUG then
			print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " claimed " .. countryName)
		end

		if CountryClaimedEvent then
			CountryClaimedEvent:FireAllClients(countryName, player.Name)
		end

		TileManager.updatePlayerCountryCache(player, countryName)

		local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")

		local countryStat = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Country")
		if countryStat then
			countryStat.Value = countryName
		end

		-- Inherit resources (coins saved when previous player left)
		local coins = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
		if coins then
			local countryCoins = ServerState.getCountryCoins(countryName)
			coins.Value = countryCoins
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " inherited " .. countryCoins .. " coins from " .. countryName)
			end
		end

		local manpower = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Manpower")
		if manpower then
			local countryManpower = ServerState.getCountryManpower(countryName)
			manpower.Value = countryManpower
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " inherited " .. countryManpower .. " manpower from " .. countryName)
			end
		end

		-- Transfer NPCs to new player (they inherit country's army)
		local npcCount = transferCountryNPCs(countryName, player)
		if npcCount > 0 and DEBUG then
			print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " inherited " .. npcCount .. " NPCs from " .. countryName)
		end

		-- Notify about inherited wars
		local enemies = DiplomacyManager.getEnemies(countryName)
		if #enemies > 0 then
			if DEBUG then
				print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " inherits wars against: " .. table.concat(enemies, ", "))
			end
			local GlobalNotificationEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GlobalNotificationEvent")
			if GlobalNotificationEvent then
				GlobalNotificationEvent:FireClient(player, "⚠️ You are at war with: " .. table.concat(enemies, ", "), Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100))
			end
		end

		-- Notify about inherited occupied territory
		local TileOwnershipManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileOwnershipManager", 10))
		local occupiedCount = TileOwnershipManager.getCountryOccupiedCount(countryName)
		if occupiedCount > 0 and DEBUG then
			print("[CountryManager] " .. player.Name .. " inherits " .. occupiedCount .. " occupied tiles")
		end

		if not loopRunning.CoinLoopRunning then
			loopRunning.CoinLoopRunning = true
			task.spawn(startCoinIncomeLoop)
		end

		if not loopRunning.ManpowerLoopRunning then
			loopRunning.ManpowerLoopRunning = true
			task.spawn(startManpowerIncomeLoop)
		end

		local capitalCFrame = getCapitalCFrame(countryName)
		if capitalCFrame and player.Character then
			player.Character:PivotTo(capitalCFrame)
		end

		-- NOTE: CountryClaimedEvent is already fired at line 348, removed duplicate here

		local playerGui = player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		if playerGui then
			local gui = playerGui:FindFirstChild(COUNTRY_SELECTION_GUI_NAME)
			if gui then
				gui.Enabled = false
			end

			local buyGui = playerGui:FindFirstChild("BuyNPCGui")
			if buyGui and buyGui:FindFirstChild("MainFrame") then
				buyGui.MainFrame.Visible = true
				buyGui.Enabled = true
			end
		end
	end)

	if claimSucceeded then
		playerClaimTime[player] = os.clock()
	end

	playerClaiming[player] = nil

	if not success then
		if claimedCountryName and CountryOwners[claimedCountryName] == player then
			CountryOwners[claimedCountryName] = "Unowned"
			ServerState.setCountryOwners(CountryOwners)
			TileManager.updatePlayerCountryCache(player, nil)
			warn("[CountryManager] Rolled back failed claim of " .. claimedCountryName)
		end
		if DEBUG then
			print("[CountryManager] Country selection failed: " .. tostring(errorMsg))
		end
	end
end

local function spawnStarterNPCs()
	-- Fixed threshold: >= 10,000 manpower gets DefenderNPC, < 10,000 gets AttackerNPC
	local DEFENDER_MANPOWER_THRESHOLD = 10000

	-- Spawn one starter NPC at each country's capital
	for _, countryModel in ipairs(EUROPE_MAP:GetChildren()) do
		if not countryModel:IsA("Model") then continue end
		local countryName = countryModel.Name

		local capitalPart = TileManager.getCountryCapital(countryName)
		if not capitalPart then
			warn("[CountryManager] No capital found for " .. countryName .. ", skipping starter NPC")
			continue
		end

		local manpower = ServerState.getCountryManpower(countryName) or 0
		local npcType = (manpower >= DEFENDER_MANPOWER_THRESHOLD) and "DefenderNPC" or "AttackerNPC"

		local spawnPos = capitalPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, capitalPart.Size.Y / 2 + 3, 0)
		local tileKey = TileManager.getTileKeyFromPart(capitalPart)

		if not tileKey then
			warn("[CountryManager] Could not get tile key for capital of " .. countryName .. ", skipping starter NPC")
			continue
		end

		NPCSpawner.spawnNPC(countryName, npcType, spawnPos, tileKey, nil) -- nil = country-owned
		if DEBUG then
			print("[CountryManager] Spawned starter " .. npcType .. " for " .. countryName .. " (manpower: " .. manpower .. ")")
		end
	end
end

local function initializeCountries()
	for _, countryModel in ipairs(EUROPE_MAP:GetChildren()) do
		if countryModel:IsA("Model") then
			CountryOwners[countryModel.Name] = "Unowned"
		end
	end
	ServerState.setCountryOwners(CountryOwners)

	local startingManpowerValues = calculateAllStartingManpower()

	for countryName, _ in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		ServerState.initializeCountryCoins(countryName, STARTING_COINS)
		local manpower = startingManpowerValues[countryName] or 20000
		ServerState.initializeCountryManpower(countryName, manpower)
	end

	isInitialized = true

	-- Spawn one starter NPC at each country's capital
	task.defer(spawnStarterNPCs)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Setup
---------------------------------------------------

local SelectCountryEvent = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("SelectCountryEvent", 10)
-- GetAvailableCountries handler was registered early (top of script) to prevent InvokeServer hangs.
local InitializationComplete = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("InitializationComplete", 10)

SelectCountryEvent.OnServerEvent:Connect(handleCountrySelection)

Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
	player.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function(character)
		onCharacterRemoving(player, character)
	end)

	-- Fire InitializationComplete every time the character spawns if the player
	-- doesn't own a country.  This covers:
	--   • Late joiners (who missed the initial FireAllClients)
	--   • Respawns after death/reset (where releasePlayerCountries already ran
	--     in CharacterRemoving, but the client's fresh LocalScript may have read
	--     the old Country stat before replication caught up)
	player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
		if not isInitialized then return end

		-- Defer so that releasePlayerCountries (from CharacterRemoving) has
		-- finished updating CountryOwners before we check.
		task.defer(function()
			-- If the player left the game during the defer, bail out
			if not player.Parent then return end

			local ownsCountry = false
			for _, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
				if owner == player then
					ownsCountry = true
					break
				end
			end

			if not ownsCountry then
				InitializationComplete:FireClient(player)
			end
		end)
	end)
end)

for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
	player.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function(character)
		onCharacterRemoving(player, character)
	end)
end

Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
	releasePlayerCountries(player, "left the game")
	playerClaiming[player] = nil
	playerClaimTime[player] = nil
end)

initializeCountries()
InitializationComplete:FireAllClients()

if DEBUG then
	print("DEBUG: Map setup complete. CountryOwners table populated.")
end
--- src/shared/TileManager.luau ---
-- TileManager (ModuleScript)
-- Now uses centralized TileKeyUtils for consistent tile key generation
-- Added: Global tile occupation tracking for movement system
-- Added: Helper functions for checking tile occupation by player
-- TileId is 100% authoritative for all occupancy reads and writes.
-- Positional key maps (GlobalOccupiedTiles, OccupiedTiles[country][key])
-- are DEBUG mirrors only — never read by gameplay logic.

local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local EUROPE_MAP = Workspace:WaitForChild("EuropeMap", 10)

local TileManager = {}
local DEBUG = false
local ServerState = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("ServerState", 10))

-- FIX: Use centralized tile key utility
local TileKeyUtils = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileKeyUtils", 10))

-- Lazy-load dependencies to avoid circular requires
local TileOwnershipManager = nil
local function getTileOwnershipManager()
	if not TileOwnershipManager then
		TileOwnershipManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileOwnershipManager", 10))
	end
	return TileOwnershipManager
end

local TileAdjacencyManager = nil
local function getTileAdjacencyManager()
	if not TileAdjacencyManager then
		TileAdjacencyManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileAdjacencyManager", 10))
	end
	return TileAdjacencyManager
end

-- VALID TILES CACHE: { [countryName] = { Vector3, Vector3, ... } }
local ValidTiles = {}

-- OCCUPIED TILES (by country): { [countryName] = { [tileId] = npcModel } }
-- Now keyed by tileId (not positional tileKey).
local OccupiedTiles = {}

-- DEBUG MIRROR — positional-key global table.
-- MUST NOT be read by gameplay logic. Maintained only for debugging convenience.
-- All occupancy reads must use GlobalOccupiedTilesById.
local GlobalOccupiedTiles = {} -- DEBUG ONLY — not read by gameplay logic

-- AUTHORITATIVE global occupancy map: { [tileId] = npcModel }
-- This is the ONLY table that gameplay logic reads for occupancy.
local GlobalOccupiedTilesById = {}

-- Tile statistics for manpower calculation
-- { [countryName] = { tileCount = N, totalArea = X, avgArea = Y } }
local CountryTileStats = {}

-- Player → Country cache for O(1) lookups
-- { [Player] = countryName }
local PlayerCountryCache = {}

-- FIX: Capital tile registry (keyed by country Model instance for immutability)
-- { [countryModel] = capitalTilePart }
local CapitalTilesByModel = {}

---------------------------------------------------
-- FIX: Use centralized getTileKey function
---------------------------------------------------
local function getTileKey(position)
	return TileKeyUtils.getTileKey(position)
end

-- Expose getTileKey for external use (delegates to TileKeyUtils)
function TileManager.getTileKey(position)
	return TileKeyUtils.getTileKey(position)
end

-- Get the tile key from a BasePart (tile)
function TileManager.getTileKeyFromPart(tilePart)
	return TileKeyUtils.getTileKeyFromPart(tilePart)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Initialization: Scan actual tile parts
---------------------------------------------------
local function scanCountryTiles(countryModel)
	local countryName = countryModel.Name
	ValidTiles[countryName] = {}
	OccupiedTiles[countryName] = {}

	local validCount = 0
	local capitalPos = nil
	local totalArea = 0

	-- Scan all BaseParts inside the country
	for _, part in ipairs(countryModel:GetDescendants()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") then
			local spawnPos = part.Position + Vector3.new(0, part.Size.Y / 2 + 3, 0)

			-- Calculate tile footprint area (X * Z)
			local tileArea = part.Size.X * part.Size.Z
			totalArea = totalArea + tileArea

			if part.Name == "Capital" then
				-- Store capital position separately
				capitalPos = spawnPos
				-- FIX: Register this tile as the country's capital (keyed by Model instance)
				CapitalTilesByModel[countryModel] = part
			else
				table.insert(ValidTiles[countryName], spawnPos)
			end
			validCount += 1
		end
	end

	-- Insert Capital at the FRONT so it's used first
	if capitalPos then
		table.insert(ValidTiles[countryName], 1, capitalPos)
	end

	-- FALLBACK: If no parts found, use model center
	if validCount == 0 then
		local center = countryModel:GetPivot().Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
		table.insert(ValidTiles[countryName], center)
		validCount = 1
		totalArea = 100 -- Default area for fallback
		if DEBUG then print(string.format("[TileManager] %s: Using center fallback (1 tile)", countryName)) end
	else
		if DEBUG then print(string.format("[TileManager] %s: %d valid tiles found, total area: %.0f", countryName, validCount, totalArea)) end
	end

	-- Store tile statistics
	CountryTileStats[countryName] = {
		tileCount = validCount,
		totalArea = totalArea,
		avgArea = totalArea / validCount
	}
end

local function initializeAllCountries()
	for _, countryModel in ipairs(EUROPE_MAP:GetChildren()) do
		if countryModel:IsA("Model") then
			scanCountryTiles(countryModel)
		end
	end
	if DEBUG then print("[TileManager] All countries scanned.") end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Tile Statistics API
---------------------------------------------------

function TileManager.getCountryTileStats(countryName)
	return CountryTileStats[countryName]
end

function TileManager.getAllCountryTileStats()
	return CountryTileStats
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Cache Management Functions
---------------------------------------------------

function TileManager.updatePlayerCountryCache(player, countryName)
	if countryName then
		PlayerCountryCache[player] = countryName
		if DEBUG then print(string.format("[TileManager] Cache updated: %s -> %s", player.Name, countryName)) end
	else
		PlayerCountryCache[player] = nil
		if DEBUG then print(string.format("[TileManager] Cache cleared for: %s", player.Name)) end
	end
end

function TileManager.clearPlayerCache(player)
	PlayerCountryCache[player] = nil
end

function TileManager.rebuildCache()
	PlayerCountryCache = {}
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	for countryName, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		if typeof(owner) == "Instance" and owner:IsA("Player") then
			PlayerCountryCache[owner] = countryName
		end
	end
	if DEBUG then print("[TileManager] Cache rebuilt from ServerState") end
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Core API
---------------------------------------------------

function TileManager.getSpawnPosition(player)
	local countryName = TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	if not countryName then return nil end

	local tiles = ValidTiles[countryName]
	if not tiles or #tiles == 0 then return nil end

	local TOM = getTileOwnershipManager()
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()

	local function getSafeSpawnPos(tilePart, fallbackPos)
		if tilePart then
			local safeCenter = TAM.getSafeCenter(tilePart)
			if safeCenter then return safeCenter end
		end
		return fallbackPos
	end

	-- Check if a tile is occupied by an enemy country (diplomatic occupation, not NPC occupancy)
	local function isEnemyDiplomaticOccupied(tilePart)
		if not tilePart then return false end
		if TOM.isOccupied(tilePart) and not TOM.isOccupiedByCountry(tilePart, countryName) then
			return true
		end
		return false
	end

	-- TIER 1: Own capital — highest priority
	-- CapitalTilesByModel is populated by scanCountryTiles at startup; direct reference, no scan needed.
	local countryModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
	local capitalPart = countryModel and CapitalTilesByModel[countryModel]
	if capitalPart then
		local capitalTileId = TAM.getTileId(capitalPart)
		if not TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(capitalTileId) and not isEnemyDiplomaticOccupied(capitalPart) then
			local fallback = capitalPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, capitalPart.Size.Y / 2 + 3, 0)
			return getSafeSpawnPos(capitalPart, fallback), getTileKey(capitalPart.Position)
		end
	end

	-- TIER 2: Conquered enemy capitals — second priority
	-- getCountryOccupiedTiles returns BaseParts from diplomatically occupied enemy territory.
	-- Parts named "Capital" within that set are the enemy's capital tiles.
	local conqueredTiles = TOM.getCountryOccupiedTiles(countryName)
	for _, tilePart in ipairs(conqueredTiles) do
		if tilePart and tilePart.Parent and tilePart.Name == "Capital" then
			local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
			if not TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId) then
				local fallback = tilePart.Position + Vector3.new(0, tilePart.Size.Y / 2 + 3, 0)
				return getSafeSpawnPos(tilePart, fallback), getTileKey(tilePart.Position)
			end
		end
	end

	-- TIER 3: All remaining eligible tiles (home + conquered), shuffled for variety.
	-- Own capital and enemy capitals that reached here are occupied, so the NPC-occupancy
	-- filter below naturally excludes them — no explicit skip logic needed.
	local allCandidates = {}

	-- Home tiles: filter out NPC-occupied tiles (by TileId) and enemy diplomatic occupants
	for _, tilePos in ipairs(tiles) do
		local tileKey = getTileKey(tilePos)
		local tilePart = TAM.getTileFromKey(tileKey)
		local tileId = tilePart and TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
		if not TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId) and not isEnemyDiplomaticOccupied(tilePart) then
			table.insert(allCandidates, { tilePart = tilePart, tileKey = tileKey, pos = tilePos })
		end
	end

	-- Conquered tiles: filter by TileId occupancy
	for _, tilePart in ipairs(conqueredTiles) do
		if tilePart and tilePart.Parent then
			local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
			if not TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId) then
				local spawnPos = tilePart.Position + Vector3.new(0, tilePart.Size.Y / 2 + 3, 0)
				local tileKey = getTileKey(tilePart.Position)
				table.insert(allCandidates, { tilePart = tilePart, tileKey = tileKey, pos = spawnPos })
			end
		end
	end

	if #allCandidates == 0 then
		warn("[TileManager] " .. countryName .. " is full!")
		return nil
	end

	-- Shuffle Tier 3 candidates for variety
	for i = #allCandidates, 2, -1 do
		local j = math.random(1, i)
		allCandidates[i], allCandidates[j] = allCandidates[j], allCandidates[i]
	end

	local chosen = allCandidates[1]
	return getSafeSpawnPos(chosen.tilePart, chosen.pos), chosen.tileKey
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Authoritative Occupancy API (TileId-based)
-- These are the preferred low-level occupancy functions.
-- All other occupancy functions must delegate to these.
---------------------------------------------------

-- PRIMARY: Occupy a tile using a pre-resolved tilePart.
-- Always writes to GlobalOccupiedTilesById (authoritative) and OccupiedTiles[country] (by tileId).
-- GlobalOccupiedTiles is updated as a DEBUG mirror only.
function TileManager.occupyResolvedTile(countryName, tilePart, npcModel)
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
	if not tileId then
		warn("[TileManager] occupyResolvedTile: no TileId for part '" .. tilePart.Name .. "' — occupancy not registered")
		return
	end

	-- Authoritative write
	GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId] = npcModel

	-- Country-local write (keyed by tileId, not positional key)
	if countryName then
		if not OccupiedTiles[countryName] then
			OccupiedTiles[countryName] = {}
		end
		OccupiedTiles[countryName][tileId] = npcModel
	end

	-- DEBUG mirror: update positional-key map for tooling/inspection
	GlobalOccupiedTiles[getTileKey(tilePart.Position)] = npcModel
end

-- PRIMARY: Release a tile using a pre-resolved tilePart.
function TileManager.releaseResolvedTile(countryName, tilePart)
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
	if not tileId then
		warn("[TileManager] releaseResolvedTile: no TileId for part '" .. tilePart.Name .. "' — occupancy not cleared")
		return
	end

	-- Authoritative clear
	GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId] = nil

	-- Country-local clear
	if countryName and OccupiedTiles[countryName] then
		OccupiedTiles[countryName][tileId] = nil
	end

	-- DEBUG mirror
	GlobalOccupiedTiles[getTileKey(tilePart.Position)] = nil
end

-- Occupy a tile by tileId directly (lowest-level write, no resolution needed).
function TileManager.occupyTileById(tileId, npcModel)
	if not tileId then return end
	GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId] = npcModel
end

-- Release a tile by tileId directly.
function TileManager.releaseTileById(tileId)
	if not tileId then return end
	GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId] = nil
end

-- Get the NPC occupying a tile by tileId (authoritative read).
function TileManager.getTileOccupantById(tileId)
	if not tileId then return nil end
	return GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId]
end

-- Check if a tile is occupied by tileId (authoritative read).
function TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId)
	if not tileId then return false end
	return GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId] ~= nil
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Compatibility Shims (tileKey-based)
-- These resolve tilePart from the legacy tileKey and delegate to the
-- TileId-authoritative functions above. Use only when tilePart is not already available.
---------------------------------------------------

-- Resolve tilePart from tileKey (tries primary lookup then fallback).
local function resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tilePart = TAM.getTileFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart and TAM.getTileFromKeyWithFallback then
		tilePart = TAM.getTileFromKeyWithFallback(tileKey)
	end
	return tilePart
end

-- Compatibility shim: resolves tilePart from tileKey, then calls occupyResolvedTile.
-- Prefer occupyResolvedTile when tilePart is already available.
function TileManager.occupyTile(countryName, tileKey, npcModel)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then
		warn("[TileManager] occupyTile: could not resolve tilePart for key '" .. tostring(tileKey) .. "' — occupancy not registered")
		return
	end
	TileManager.occupyResolvedTile(countryName, tilePart, npcModel)
end

-- Compatibility shim: resolves tilePart from tileKey, then calls releaseResolvedTile.
-- Prefer releaseResolvedTile when tilePart is already available.
function TileManager.releaseTile(countryName, tileKey)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then
		warn("[TileManager] releaseTile: could not resolve tilePart for key '" .. tostring(tileKey) .. "' — occupancy not cleared")
		return
	end
	TileManager.releaseResolvedTile(countryName, tilePart)
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Global Tile Occupation (for movement system)
---------------------------------------------------

-- Occupy a tile globally (regardless of country).
-- Compatibility shim: resolves tilePart and country from tileKey/npcModel, then calls occupyResolvedTile.
-- Prefer occupyResolvedTile with an explicit countryName when possible.
function TileManager.occupyTileGlobal(tileKey, npcModel)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then
		warn("[TileManager] occupyTileGlobal: could not resolve tilePart for key '" .. tostring(tileKey) .. "'")
		return
	end
	local npcCountry = npcModel:GetAttribute("Country")
	TileManager.occupyResolvedTile(npcCountry, tilePart, npcModel)
end

-- Release a tile globally.
-- Compatibility shim: resolves tilePart and country, then calls releaseResolvedTile.
function TileManager.releaseTileGlobal(tileKey)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then
		-- Fallback: clear DEBUG mirror at least
		GlobalOccupiedTiles[tileKey] = nil
		warn("[TileManager] releaseTileGlobal: could not resolve tilePart for key '" .. tostring(tileKey) .. "'")
		return
	end
	-- Determine country from authoritative occupant
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
	local npcModel = (tileId and GlobalOccupiedTilesById[tileId]) or GlobalOccupiedTiles[tileKey]
	local npcCountry = npcModel and npcModel:GetAttribute("Country")
	TileManager.releaseResolvedTile(npcCountry, tilePart)
end

-- Check if a tile is occupied globally (TileId-authoritative).
-- Compatibility shim for callers that only have a tileKey.
function TileManager.isTileOccupied(tileKey)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then return false end
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
	return TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId)
end

-- Get the NPC occupying a tile (TileId-authoritative).
-- Compatibility shim for callers that only have a tileKey.
function TileManager.getTileOccupant(tileKey)
	local tilePart = resolveTilePartFromKey(tileKey)
	if not tilePart then return nil end
	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local tileId = TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
	return TileManager.getTileOccupantById(tileId)
end

-- Check if a tile is occupied by a specific player's NPC (TileId-authoritative).
function TileManager.isTileOccupiedByPlayer(tileKey, player)
	local npc = TileManager.getTileOccupant(tileKey)
	if not npc then return false end

	local ownerVal = npc:FindFirstChild("NPCOwner")
	if ownerVal and ownerVal.Value == player then
		return true
	end

	return false
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Existing API
---------------------------------------------------

function TileManager.getAvailableTileCount(countryName)
	local tiles = ValidTiles[countryName]
	if not tiles then return 0 end

	local TAM = getTileAdjacencyManager()
	local available = 0
	for _, tilePos in ipairs(tiles) do
		local tileKey = getTileKey(tilePos)
		local tilePart = TAM.getTileFromKey(tileKey)
		local tileId = tilePart and TAM.getTileId(tilePart)
		-- isTileOccupiedById returns false for nil tileId (counts unresolvable tiles as available)
		if not TileManager.isTileOccupiedById(tileId) then
			available += 1
		end
	end
	return available
end

function TileManager.getPlayerCountry(player)
	-- First, try the cache (O(1) lookup)
	local cachedCountry = PlayerCountryCache[player]
	if cachedCountry then
		-- Verify it's still valid (in case ServerState changed without cache update)
		local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
		if CountryOwners[cachedCountry] == player then
			return cachedCountry
		else
			-- Cache is stale, clear it
			PlayerCountryCache[player] = nil
		end
	end

	-- Fallback: iterate through all countries (O(n) but only on cache miss)
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	for countryName, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		if owner == player then
			-- Update cache for next time
			PlayerCountryCache[player] = countryName
			return countryName
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function TileManager.getCountryModel(countryName)
	return EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
end

function TileManager.getAvailableCountries()
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()
	local list = {}
	for countryName, owner in pairs(CountryOwners) do
		if owner == "Unowned" then
			table.insert(list, countryName)
		end
	end
	return list
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- FIX: Capital Tile Registry API
---------------------------------------------------

-- Get the capital tile for a country by its Model instance (primary API)
function TileManager.getCountryCapitalByModel(countryModel)
	return CapitalTilesByModel[countryModel]
end

-- Get the capital tile for a country by name (convenience wrapper)
function TileManager.getCountryCapital(countryName)
	local countryModel = EUROPE_MAP:FindFirstChild(countryName)
	if not countryModel then return nil end
	return CapitalTilesByModel[countryModel]
end

---------------------------------------------------
-- Player Cleanup
---------------------------------------------------

Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
	TileManager.clearPlayerCache(player)
end)

initializeAllCountries()

return TileManager

--- src/shared/DiplomacyManager.luau ---
-- DiplomacyManager
-- Added duplicate war declaration prevention
-- Wars persist when players leave - new player inherits wars
-- Added country-level war checks for NPC combat
-- NAPs are now timed truces: stored as os.clock() expiration timestamps

local DiplomacyManager = {}
local DEBUG = false
local ServerState = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("ServerState", 10))
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Default NAP duration in seconds (5 minutes)
local DEFAULT_NAP_DURATION = 300

-- Lazy load to avoid circular dependency
local TileManager = nil
local function getTileManager()
	if not TileManager then
		TileManager = require(game:GetService("ServerScriptService"):WaitForChild("TileManager", 10))
	end
	return TileManager
end

-- Data Structure:
-- Wars["France"] = { ["Germany"] = true }
-- Alliances["France"] = { ["Germany"] = true }
-- NonAggressionPacts["France"] = { ["Germany"] = <os.clock() expiration timestamp> }
local Wars = {}
local Alliances = {}
local NonAggressionPacts = {}

function DiplomacyManager.initCountry(countryName)
	if not Wars[countryName] then
		Wars[countryName] = {}
	end
	if not Alliances[countryName] then
		Alliances[countryName] = {}
	end
	if not NonAggressionPacts[countryName] then
		NonAggressionPacts[countryName] = {}
	end
end

-- Check if two COUNTRIES are at war (not players)
function DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end
	if countryA == countryB then return false end

	return (Wars[countryA] and Wars[countryA][countryB] == true) or false
end

-- Check if two COUNTRIES are allied
function DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end
	if countryA == countryB then return true end

	return (Alliances[countryA] and Alliances[countryA][countryB] == true) or false
end

-- Check if two COUNTRIES have a Non-Aggression Pact (timed truce)
-- Returns true only if a pact exists AND has not yet expired
function DiplomacyManager.hasNonAggressionPact(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end
	if countryA == countryB then return true end

	local expiresAt = NonAggressionPacts[countryA] and NonAggressionPacts[countryA][countryB]
	if type(expiresAt) == "number" and expiresAt > os.clock() then
		return true
	end

	return false
end

-- Get the remaining time (in seconds) on a NAP between two countries
-- Returns 0 if no active pact exists
function DiplomacyManager.getNAPTimeRemaining(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return 0 end
	if countryA == countryB then return 0 end

	local expiresAt = NonAggressionPacts[countryA] and NonAggressionPacts[countryA][countryB]
	if type(expiresAt) == "number" then
		local remaining = expiresAt - os.clock()
		if remaining > 0 then
			return remaining
		end
	end

	return 0
end

-- Get the absolute expiration timestamp for a NAP (for sending to clients)
-- Returns nil if no active pact exists
function DiplomacyManager.getNAPExpiresAt(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return nil end
	if countryA == countryB then return nil end

	local expiresAt = NonAggressionPacts[countryA] and NonAggressionPacts[countryA][countryB]
	if type(expiresAt) == "number" and expiresAt > os.clock() then
		return expiresAt
	end

	return nil
end

-- Declare War - Returns false if already at war
function DiplomacyManager.declareWar(attackerCountry, defenderCountry)
	if not attackerCountry or not defenderCountry then
		return false, "Invalid countries"
	end

	if attackerCountry == defenderCountry then
		return false, "Cannot declare war on yourself"
	end

	if DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(attackerCountry, defenderCountry) then
		return false, "Already at war"
	end

	if DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(attackerCountry, defenderCountry) then
		return false, "You are allied. Break the alliance first."
	end

	if DiplomacyManager.hasNonAggressionPact(attackerCountry, defenderCountry) then
		return false, "A Non-Aggression Pact is active. Break it first."
	end

	if not Wars[attackerCountry] then DiplomacyManager.initCountry(attackerCountry) end
	if not Wars[defenderCountry] then DiplomacyManager.initCountry(defenderCountry) end

	-- Break any existing alliance or NAP first (safeguard)
	if Alliances[attackerCountry] then Alliances[attackerCountry][defenderCountry] = nil end
	if Alliances[defenderCountry] then Alliances[defenderCountry][attackerCountry] = nil end
	if NonAggressionPacts[attackerCountry] then NonAggressionPacts[attackerCountry][defenderCountry] = nil end
	if NonAggressionPacts[defenderCountry] then NonAggressionPacts[defenderCountry][attackerCountry] = nil end

	-- War is mutual
	Wars[attackerCountry][defenderCountry] = true
	Wars[defenderCountry][attackerCountry] = true

	if DEBUG then print("WAR DECLARED: " .. attackerCountry .. " vs " .. defenderCountry) end
	return true, "War declared"
end

-- Make Peace
function DiplomacyManager.makePeace(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end

	if Wars[countryA] then Wars[countryA][countryB] = nil end
	if Wars[countryB] then Wars[countryB][countryA] = nil end
	if DEBUG then print("PEACE SIGNED: " .. countryA .. " and " .. countryB) end
	return true
end

-- Clear all wars for a country (called when country is conquered)
function DiplomacyManager.clearAllWarsForCountry(countryName)
	if not countryName then return end

	local enemies = {}
	if Wars[countryName] then
		for enemy, atWar in pairs(Wars[countryName]) do
			if atWar then
				table.insert(enemies, enemy)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Remove bilateral war entries
	for _, enemy in ipairs(enemies) do
		if Wars[enemy] then
			Wars[enemy][countryName] = nil
		end
	end

	-- Clear the conquered country's wars table
	Wars[countryName] = {}

	if DEBUG then print("WARS CLEARED: " .. countryName .. " (was at war with " .. #enemies .. " countries)") end
end

-- Clear all alliances for a country (called when country is conquered)
function DiplomacyManager.clearAllAlliancesForCountry(countryName)
	if not countryName then return end

	local allies = {}
	if Alliances[countryName] then
		for ally, isAllied in pairs(Alliances[countryName]) do
			if isAllied then
				table.insert(allies, ally)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Remove bilateral alliance entries
	for _, ally in ipairs(allies) do
		if Alliances[ally] then
			Alliances[ally][countryName] = nil
		end
	end

	-- Clear the conquered country's alliances table
	Alliances[countryName] = {}

	if DEBUG then print("ALLIANCES CLEARED: " .. countryName .. " (was allied with " .. #allies .. " countries)") end
end

-- Clear all NAPs for a country (called when country is conquered)
function DiplomacyManager.clearAllNAPsForCountry(countryName)
	if not countryName then return end

	local partners = {}
	if NonAggressionPacts[countryName] then
		for partner, expiresAt in pairs(NonAggressionPacts[countryName]) do
			if type(expiresAt) == "number" then
				table.insert(partners, partner)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Remove bilateral NAP entries
	for _, partner in ipairs(partners) do
		if NonAggressionPacts[partner] then
			NonAggressionPacts[partner][countryName] = nil
		end
	end

	-- Clear the conquered country's NAPs table
	NonAggressionPacts[countryName] = {}

	if DEBUG then print("NAPS CLEARED: " .. countryName .. " (had NAPs with " .. #partners .. " countries)") end
end

-- Clear ALL diplomacy for a country (wars, alliances, NAPs) — single call for conquest cleanup
function DiplomacyManager.clearAllDiplomacyForCountry(countryName)
	if not countryName then return end

	DiplomacyManager.clearAllWarsForCountry(countryName)
	DiplomacyManager.clearAllAlliancesForCountry(countryName)
	DiplomacyManager.clearAllNAPsForCountry(countryName)

	if DEBUG then print("ALL DIPLOMACY CLEARED: " .. countryName) end
end

-- Get country from player OR from NPC's country attribute
local function getEntityCountry(entity)
	if not entity then return nil end

	if typeof(entity) == "Instance" and entity:IsA("Player") then
		return getTileManager().getPlayerCountry(entity)
	end

	if type(entity) == "string" then
		return entity
	end

	return nil
end

-- CHECK: Are these two players at war? (checks their countries)
function DiplomacyManager.areAtWar(playerA, playerB)
	if not playerA or not playerB then
		return false
	end

	if playerA == playerB then
		return false
	end

	local countryA = getEntityCountry(playerA)
	local countryB = getEntityCountry(playerB)

	if not countryA or not countryB then
		return false
	end

	return DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(countryA, countryB)
end

-- Check if an NPC's country is at war with another NPC's country
-- This works even when countries are unowned
function DiplomacyManager.areNPCsAtWar(npcA, npcB)
	if not npcA or not npcB then return false end

	local countryA = npcA:GetAttribute("Country")
	local countryB = npcB:GetAttribute("Country")

	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end

	return DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(countryA, countryB)
end

-- Check if NPC can attack based on country-level diplomacy
function DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(attackerNPC, targetNPC)
	if not attackerNPC or not targetNPC then return false end

	local attackerCountry = attackerNPC:GetAttribute("Country")
	local targetCountry = targetNPC:GetAttribute("Country")

	if not attackerCountry or not targetCountry then return false end

	-- Same country = no friendly fire
	if attackerCountry == targetCountry then
		return false
	end

	-- Check if allied
	if DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(attackerCountry, targetCountry) then
		return false
	end

	-- Must be at war
	return DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAtWar(attackerCountry, targetCountry)
end

-- FORM ALLIANCE
function DiplomacyManager.formAlliance(countryA, countryB)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end
	if countryA == countryB then return false end

	if not Alliances[countryA] then Alliances[countryA] = {} end
	if not Alliances[countryB] then Alliances[countryB] = {} end

	Alliances[countryA][countryB] = true
	Alliances[countryB][countryA] = true

	DiplomacyManager.makePeace(countryA, countryB)

	if DEBUG then print("ALLIANCE FORMED: " .. countryA .. " and " .. countryB) end
	return true
end

-- Break Alliance
function DiplomacyManager.breakAlliance(countryA, countryB)
	if Alliances[countryA] then Alliances[countryA][countryB] = nil end
	if Alliances[countryB] then Alliances[countryB][countryA] = nil end
	if DEBUG then print("ALLIANCE BROKEN: " .. countryA .. " and " .. countryB) end
end

-- FORM NON-AGGRESSION PACT (timed truce)
-- duration: seconds until the pact expires (defaults to DEFAULT_NAP_DURATION)
function DiplomacyManager.formNonAggressionPact(countryA, countryB, duration)
	if not countryA or not countryB then return false end
	if countryA == countryB then return false end

	duration = duration or DEFAULT_NAP_DURATION
	local expiresAt = os.clock() + duration

	if not NonAggressionPacts[countryA] then NonAggressionPacts[countryA] = {} end
	if not NonAggressionPacts[countryB] then NonAggressionPacts[countryB] = {} end

	NonAggressionPacts[countryA][countryB] = expiresAt
	NonAggressionPacts[countryB][countryA] = expiresAt

	DiplomacyManager.makePeace(countryA, countryB)

	if DEBUG then print("NAP FORMED: " .. countryA .. " and " .. countryB .. " (expires in " .. duration .. "s)") end
	return true
end

-- BREAK NON-AGGRESSION PACT (manual break by a player)
function DiplomacyManager.breakNonAggressionPact(countryA, countryB)
	if NonAggressionPacts[countryA] then NonAggressionPacts[countryA][countryB] = nil end
	if NonAggressionPacts[countryB] then NonAggressionPacts[countryB][countryA] = nil end
	if DEBUG then print("NAP BROKEN: " .. countryA .. " and " .. countryB) end
end

-- CHECK ALLIANCE
function DiplomacyManager.areAllied(playerA, playerB)
	if not playerA or not playerB then
		return false
	end

	if playerA == playerB then
		return true
	end

	local countryA = getEntityCountry(playerA)
	local countryB = getEntityCountry(playerB)

	if not countryA or not countryB then
		return false
	end

	return DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(countryA, countryB)
end

-- Legacy canAttack for player-based checks
function DiplomacyManager.canAttack(attackerOwner, targetOwner)
	if attackerOwner and targetOwner and attackerOwner == targetOwner then
		return false
	end

	if not attackerOwner or not targetOwner then
		return false
	end

	if DiplomacyManager.areAllied(attackerOwner, targetOwner) then
		return false
	end

	return DiplomacyManager.areAtWar(attackerOwner, targetOwner)
end

-- Get all countries at war with a given country
-- Filter out conquered countries from the enemy list
function DiplomacyManager.getEnemies(countryName)
	local enemies = {}
	local CountryOwners = ServerState.getCountryOwners()

	if Wars[countryName] then
		for enemy, atWar in pairs(Wars[countryName]) do
			if atWar then
				-- Filter out conquered countries
				local enemyOwner = CountryOwners[enemy]
				local isConquered = type(enemyOwner) == "string" and enemyOwner:find("Conquered_")
				if not isConquered then
					table.insert(enemies, enemy)
				end
			end
		end
	end
	return enemies
end

-- Get all allied countries
function DiplomacyManager.getAllies(countryName)
	local allies = {}
	if Alliances[countryName] then
		for ally, isAllied in pairs(Alliances[countryName]) do
			if isAllied then
				table.insert(allies, ally)
			end
		end
	end
	return allies
end

-- Get all countries with an active NAP with the given country
function DiplomacyManager.getNAPPartners(countryName)
	local partners = {}
	local now = os.clock()
	if NonAggressionPacts[countryName] then
		for partner, expiresAt in pairs(NonAggressionPacts[countryName]) do
			if type(expiresAt) == "number" and expiresAt > now then
				table.insert(partners, partner)
			end
		end
	end
	return partners
end

-- Check if a country is at war with anyone
function DiplomacyManager.isAtWarWithAnyone(countryName)
	if Wars[countryName] then
		for _, atWar in pairs(Wars[countryName]) do
			if atWar then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	return false
end

-- Debug
function DiplomacyManager.debugPrintWars()
	if not DEBUG then return end
	print("=== ACTIVE WARS ===")
	local printed = {}
	for countryA, enemies in pairs(Wars) do
		for countryB, atWar in pairs(enemies) do
			if atWar then
				local key = countryA < countryB and (countryA.."-"..countryB) or (countryB.."-"..countryA)
				if not printed[key] then
					print("  " .. countryA .. " vs " .. countryB)
					printed[key] = true
				end
			end
		end
	end
	print("===================")
end

---------------------------------------------------------
-- NAP EXPIRATION SWEEP (Server-side only)
---------------------------------------------------------
-- Runs every 5 seconds, checks all NAPs for expiration.
-- Expired pacts are removed bilaterally and a global notification is fired.
-- This only runs on the server (RunService:IsServer()).

if RunService:IsServer() then
	local NAP_SWEEP_INTERVAL = 5
	local lastSweep = os.clock()

	-- Callback for on-expiry notification (set by DiplomacyServer via setNAPExpiredCallback)
	local napExpiredCallback = nil

	function DiplomacyManager.setNAPExpiredCallback(callback)
		napExpiredCallback = callback
	end

	local sweepConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		local now = os.clock()
		if now - lastSweep < NAP_SWEEP_INTERVAL then
			return
		end
		lastSweep = now

		-- Collect expired pacts first, then remove (avoid mutating during iteration)
		local expired = {}
		local seen = {}

		for countryA, pacts in pairs(NonAggressionPacts) do
			for countryB, expiresAt in pairs(pacts) do
				if type(expiresAt) == "number" and expiresAt <= now then
					-- Deduplicate: only process each pair once
					local key = countryA < countryB and (countryA .. "|" .. countryB) or (countryB .. "|" .. countryA)
					if not seen[key] then
						seen[key] = true
						table.insert(expired, { countryA, countryB })
					end
				end
			end
		end

		-- Remove expired pacts and notify
		for _, pair in ipairs(expired) do
			local a, b = pair[1], pair[2]
			if NonAggressionPacts[a] then NonAggressionPacts[a][b] = nil end
			if NonAggressionPacts[b] then NonAggressionPacts[b][a] = nil end

			if DEBUG then print("NAP EXPIRED: " .. a .. " and " .. b) end

			-- Fire the callback so DiplomacyServer can send global notifications
			if napExpiredCallback then
				task.spawn(napExpiredCallback, a, b)
			end
		end
	end)

	-- Store connection reference for potential cleanup (module-level, not per-player)
	DiplomacyManager._sweepConnection = sweepConnection
end

return DiplomacyManager

--- src/server/NPCTargetingHandler.server.luau ---
-- NPCTargetingHandler (MULTI-TARGET + MOVEMENT VERSION)
-- Added tile click detection for NPC movement system
-- Click NPC head = select for targeting
-- With NPC selected: click enemy NPC head = attack, click tile = move

local Combat = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("NPCCombatSystem", 10))
local TileAdjacencyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileAdjacencyManager", 10))
local TileManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("TileManager", 10))
local DiplomacyManager = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("DiplomacyManager", 10))
local NPCMovementSystem = require(game.ServerScriptService:WaitForChild("NPCMovementSystem", 10))
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")

local NPC_TAG = "RegisteredNPC"

local DEBUG = false

local SelectionVisualEvent = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("SelectionVisualEvent", 10)
local NPCMoveToTileEvent = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("NPCMoveToTileEvent", 10)

local EUROPE_MAP = Workspace:WaitForChild("EuropeMap", 10)

local selectedNPC = {} -- player -> npcModel

-- Store both the flag AND the connection for proper cleanup
-- connectedNPCs[npcModel] = { connected = true, clickConnection = RBXScriptConnection }
local connectedNPCs = {}

local function getNPCModel(part)
	local model = part.Parent
	while model and not model:IsA("Model") do
		model = model.Parent
	end
	if model and model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and model:FindFirstChild("NPCOwner") then
		return model
	end
	return nil
end

-- Helper to check if a part is a tile (inside EuropeMap)
local function isTilePart(part)
	if not part or not part:IsA("BasePart") then return false end

	-- Walk up to check if this part is inside EuropeMap
	local current = part.Parent
	while current and current ~= Workspace do
		if current == EUROPE_MAP then
			return true
		end
		if current.Parent == EUROPE_MAP then
			return true
		end
		current = current.Parent
	end
	return false
end

-- Helper to get country model from a tile part
local function getTileCountryModel(part)
	local current = part.Parent
	while current and current ~= EUROPE_MAP and current ~= Workspace do
		if current.Parent == EUROPE_MAP then
			return current
		end
		current = current.Parent
	end
	return nil
end

-- Helper: Find a living NPC occupying a tile.
-- Uses TileId-authoritative lookup directly (tilePart is already available from click handler).
local function findNPCOnTile(tilePart)
	local tileId = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileId(tilePart)
	if not tileId then return nil end
	local npc = TileManager.getTileOccupantById(tileId)
	if npc and npc.Parent and npc:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
		local humanoid = npc:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if humanoid.Health > 0 then
			return npc
		end
	end
	return nil
end

-- Helper to clear selection for a player
local function clearSelection(player)
	local currentSelection = selectedNPC[player]
	if currentSelection then
		SelectionVisualEvent:FireClient(player, currentSelection, false)
		selectedNPC[player] = nil
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " deselected their unit") end
	end
end

local function handleFirstClick(player, npcModel)
	local owner = Combat.getOwner(npcModel)

	if not owner then
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " cannot select NPC: No owner registered") end
		return
	end

	-- Check if NPC is retreating (can't be selected)
	if NPCMovementSystem.isRetreating(npcModel) then
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " cannot select NPC: Currently retreating") end
		return
	end

	if owner == player then
		-- Clear old selection highlight (but keep the NPC's targets!)
		local oldNPC = selectedNPC[player]
		if oldNPC then
			SelectionVisualEvent:FireClient(player, oldNPC, false)
		end

		selectedNPC[player] = npcModel

		local targetCount = Combat.getManualTargetCount(npcModel)
		local movementState = NPCMovementSystem.getMovementState(npcModel)
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " selected: " .. npcModel.Name .. " (targeting " .. targetCount .. " enemies, state: " .. movementState .. ")") end

		SelectionVisualEvent:FireClient(player, npcModel, true)
	else
		local ownerName = "Unknown"
		if typeof(owner) == "Instance" and owner:IsA("Player") then
			ownerName = owner.Name
		elseif typeof(owner) == "Instance" then
			ownerName = owner.Name or "ServerOwned"
		end
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " cannot select NPC owned by: " .. ownerName) end
	end
end

local function handleSecondClick(player, targetModel)
	local attackerModel = selectedNPC[player]
	if not attackerModel then
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " needs to select an Attacker first.") end
		return
	end

	local attackerOwner = Combat.getOwner(attackerModel)

	-- Only require attacker to have an owner
	if not attackerOwner then
		if DEBUG then print("Cannot process attack: Your attacker has no owner") end
		return
	end

	local attackerRole = Combat.getRole(attackerModel)
	local targetRole = Combat.getRole(targetModel)

	-- Use country-based attack validation so country-owned (nil-owner) NPCs are handled correctly
	if not DiplomacyManager.canNPCAttack(attackerModel, targetModel) then
		-- Determine reason for better feedback using country attributes
		local attackerCountry = attackerModel:GetAttribute("Country")
		local targetCountry = targetModel:GetAttribute("Country")
		if attackerCountry == targetCountry then
			if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: " .. targetModel.Name .. " is owned by you") end
		elseif DiplomacyManager.areCountriesAllied(attackerCountry, targetCountry) then
			if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: " .. targetModel.Name .. " belongs to an allied country") end
		else
			if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: You are not at war with " .. targetModel.Name .. "'s country") end
		end
		return
	end

	-- Rule 2: Only Attackers can be manually directed
	if attackerRole ~= "Attacker" then
		if DEBUG then print(attackerModel.Name .. " is a Defender and cannot be manually directed to attack.") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	if NPCMovementSystem.isMoving(attackerModel) then
		if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: " .. attackerModel.Name .. " is currently moving") end
		return
	end

	-- Rule 3: Tile adjacency check
	if not TileAdjacencyManager.canNPCsInteract(attackerModel, targetModel) then
		if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: " .. targetModel.Name .. " is not on an adjacent tile") end
		return
	end

	-- Check if target is retreating (invulnerable)
	if NPCMovementSystem.isRetreating(targetModel) then
		if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: " .. targetModel.Name .. " is retreating (invulnerable)") end
		return
	end

	if NPCMovementSystem.isMoving(targetModel) then
		local restored, restoreResult = NPCMovementSystem.restoreToMovementOrigin(targetModel)
		if not restored then
			if DEBUG then print("Cannot attack: failed to restore moving target " .. targetModel.Name .. " (" .. tostring(restoreResult) .. ")") end
			return
		end
	end

	-- ADD target to the list (not replace!)
	local added = Combat.addManualTarget(attackerModel, targetModel)

	if added then
		-- Notify the target that they're being attacked (for auto-retaliation)
		if targetRole == "Defender" then
			Combat.noteAttackerTargeting(attackerModel, targetModel)
		elseif targetRole == "Attacker" then
			Combat.noteTargetingAttacker(attackerModel, targetModel)
		end

		local targetCount = Combat.getManualTargetCount(attackerModel)
		if DEBUG then print(attackerModel.Name .. " now targeting " .. targetCount .. " enemy(s) (added " .. targetModel.Name .. ")") end
	else
		if DEBUG then print(attackerModel.Name .. " is already targeting " .. targetModel.Name) end
	end

	-- Always clear selection after assigning a target
	clearSelection(player)
end

-- Handle tile click for movement
local function handleTileClick(player, tilePart)
	local npcModel = selectedNPC[player]
	if not npcModel then
		if DEBUG then print(player.Name .. " needs to select an NPC first.") end
		return
	end

	-- Check if target tile is directly adjacent before allowing movement
	-- MUST verify adjacency - block movement if we can't determine current tile
	local currentTileId = npcModel:GetAttribute("CurrentTileId")
	local currentTilePart = currentTileId and TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromId(currentTileId) or nil
	if not currentTilePart then
		local currentTileKey = npcModel:GetAttribute("TileKey")
		if not currentTileKey then
			if DEBUG then print("Movement failed: NPC has no current tile") end
			clearSelection(player)
			return
		end

		currentTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKey(currentTileKey)
		if not currentTilePart then
			currentTilePart = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileFromKeyWithFallback(currentTileKey)
		end
	end
	if not currentTilePart then
		if DEBUG then print("Movement failed: Could not resolve NPC's current tile") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	-- Validate NPC is actually near its resolved tile (prevents TileKey mismatch in small countries)
	-- If the NPC's physical position is far from the resolved tile, re-resolve from actual position
	local npcRoot = npcModel:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or npcModel.PrimaryPart
	if npcRoot and currentTilePart then
		local npcPosXZ = npcRoot.Position * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)
		local tilePosXZ = currentTilePart.Position * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)
		local tileDistance = (npcPosXZ - tilePosXZ).Magnitude

		-- If NPC is far from its attributed tile, re-resolve from physical position
		if tileDistance > currentTilePart.Size.Magnitude / 2 + 5 then
			local correctedTile = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileUnderPosition(npcRoot.Position)
			if correctedTile then
				if DEBUG then print("[Movement] TileKey mismatch corrected: " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " -> " .. correctedTile.Name .. " (NPC was " .. math.floor(tileDistance) .. " studs from attributed tile)") end
				currentTilePart = correctedTile
				-- Update the NPC's TileKey to prevent future mismatches
				local correctedKey = TileManager.getTileKeyFromPart(correctedTile)
				if correctedKey then
					npcModel:SetAttribute("TileKey", correctedKey)
				end
				-- Fix C: Update CurrentTileId to match the corrected tile
				local correctedTileId = TileAdjacencyManager.getTileId(correctedTile)
				if correctedTileId then
					npcModel:SetAttribute("CurrentTileId", correctedTileId)
				end
			end
		end
	end

	-- Add distance check as a safeguard against invalid tile resolution
	local distance = (currentTilePart.Position - tilePart.Position).Magnitude
	if distance > 100 then -- Tiles should be within reasonable distance
		if DEBUG then print("[Movement] BLOCKED: Target tile too far (" .. math.floor(distance) .. " studs)") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	-- Debug logging to help diagnose adjacency issues
	local isAdjacent = TileAdjacencyManager.areTilesAdjacent(currentTilePart, tilePart)
	if DEBUG then
		print("[Movement] " .. player.Name .. " moving from " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " to " .. tilePart.Name)
		print("[Movement] Distance: " .. math.floor(distance) .. " studs | Adjacent: " .. tostring(isAdjacent))
	end

	-- Check adjacency - must be directly adjacent (one tile away)
	if not isAdjacent then
		-- Full diagnostic when adjacency fails
		TileAdjacencyManager.diagnoseAdjacency(currentTilePart, tilePart)

		local repaired = TileAdjacencyManager.tryRepairAdjacencyPair(currentTilePart, tilePart)
		if repaired then
			isAdjacent = TileAdjacencyManager.areTilesAdjacent(currentTilePart, tilePart)
			if isAdjacent then
				if DEBUG then print(string.format("[Movement] Repaired adjacency at runtime: %s <-> %s", currentTilePart.Name, tilePart.Name)) end
			end
		else
			if DEBUG then print(string.format("[Movement] Runtime adjacency repair did not connect: %s <-> %s", currentTilePart.Name, tilePart.Name)) end
		end

		if not isAdjacent then
			if DEBUG then print("Movement failed: Target tile (" .. tilePart.Name .. ") is not adjacent to current tile (" .. currentTilePart.Name .. ")") end
			clearSelection(player)
			return
		end
	end

	-- Secondary validation: confirm a walkable crossing proof exists for this pair.
	-- areTilesAdjacent() is a lookup-only check; the proof confirms a real walkable border.
	local proof = TileAdjacencyManager.getAdjacencyProof(currentTilePart, tilePart)
	if not proof then
		if DEBUG then print("[Movement] BLOCKED: No walkable crossing proof for " .. currentTilePart.Name .. " -> " .. tilePart.Name .. " (adjacency table false positive?)") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	-- Block movement while the NPC is engaged in combat
	if Combat.isInCombat(npcModel) then
		if DEBUG then print("[Movement] " .. npcModel.Name .. " cannot move: currently engaged in combat") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	-- Check if NPC is moving (cancel current movement for new order)
	if NPCMovementSystem.isMoving(npcModel) then
		NPCMovementSystem.cancelMovement(npcModel)
	end

	-- Get tile key
	local targetTileKey = TileManager.getTileKeyFromPart(tilePart)
	if not targetTileKey then
		if DEBUG then print("Could not determine tile key for clicked part") end
		clearSelection(player)
		return
	end

	-- Attempt to move
	local success, errorMsg = NPCMovementSystem.startMovement(npcModel, targetTileKey, tilePart)

	if success then
		if DEBUG then print(npcModel.Name .. " moving to tile " .. targetTileKey) end
	else
		if DEBUG then print("Movement failed: " .. (errorMsg or "Unknown error")) end
	end

	-- Clear selection after issuing movement order
	clearSelection(player)
end

-- Disconnect and clean up NPC connections properly
local function disconnectNPC(npcModel)
	local data = connectedNPCs[npcModel]
	if data then
		if data.clickConnection then
			data.clickConnection:Disconnect()
		end
		connectedNPCs[npcModel] = nil
	end
end

local function connectNPC(npcModel)
	if connectedNPCs[npcModel] then return end

	local head = npcModel:FindFirstChild("Head")
	if not head then return end

	local clickDetector = head:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
	if not clickDetector then return end

	-- Store the connection so we can disconnect it later
	local clickConnection = clickDetector.MouseClick:Connect(function(player)
		local npc = getNPCModel(head)
		if not npc then return end

		-- Ignore dead/dying NPCs (cleanup sets Dead=true and destroys ClickDetector,
		-- but guard here as a belt-and-suspenders safety check)
		local hum = npc:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if not hum or hum.Health <= 0 or npc:GetAttribute("Dead") then return end

		-- Check if clicking your currently selected NPC (deselect)
		if selectedNPC[player] == npc then
			clearSelection(player)
			return
		end

		if selectedNPC[player] then
			handleSecondClick(player, npc)
		else
			handleFirstClick(player, npc)
		end
	end)

	-- Store both the flag and the connection
	connectedNPCs[npcModel] = {
		connected = true,
		clickConnection = clickConnection
	}

	-- Also disconnect when NPC is destroyed
	npcModel.Destroying:Once(function()
		disconnectNPC(npcModel)
	end)
end

-- Initialize existing registered NPCs
for _, npcModel in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged(NPC_TAG)) do
	connectNPC(npcModel)
end

-- Connect new NPCs when they receive the RegisteredNPC tag
CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal(NPC_TAG):Connect(function(npcModel)
	connectNPC(npcModel)
end)

-- Clean up player state when they leave
Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
	if selectedNPC[player] then
		selectedNPC[player] = nil
	end
end)

-- Clean up NPC tracking when an NPC is unregistered or destroyed
